  - `**PINNED_HASH.txt` re-pin.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt)` regenerated via `python -m xion_verify --self-test --update --i-understand` after the verifier landed. `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` green end-to-end.
  - **D2 Operations troubleshooting matrix ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `[docs/13-OPERATIONS.md](./docs/13-OPERATIONS.md)` ├é┬¦ "D2 Deploy Runbook" ├é┬¦ "Troubleshooting matrix".** The 503 row splits into seven rows ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ one per `ProviderErrorEnvelope.reason` value ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ so an operator reading a 503 at 3 am can jump from the typed class directly to the diagnostic and the fix class. `no_healthy_provider` now explicitly names the pre-selection posture ("no provider registered with `generate`") as distinct from the post-attempt typed failures.
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not change the hosted gateway (`https://openrouter.ai/api/v1`) or the Genesis Default slug (`moonshotai/kimi-k2.6` from Stage 0 stays). Did not add retry-with-backoff within an attempt (a single attempt is either success or a typed failure, and the loop advances ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ retries would widen the deadline budget and obscure the P5 classification). Did not open `KW-INFER-004` for "hosted upstream that refuses a Covenant-bounded candidate" ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `moderation_refusal` is a legitimate typed failure and the handler falls through to the floor, which is the correct posture for a deployment that believes the Arbiter is authoritative. Did not change the cost-model surface; Pay-to-Activate refunds still scope to the chat turn, not per-attempt (the turn is the unit of billing; attempts are the unit of observability).
- **D2 Deploy Runbook ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `docs/13-OPERATIONS.md` ├é┬¦ "D2 Deploy Runbook (Phase 5g+ surface)" (2026-04-23).** First operator-facing runbook that stitches every surface landed through Phase 5g+ (Invariant-17 open-weights floor, OpenRouter hosted gateway with Genesis-Default model rotation, bearer admission + per-principal sliding-window rate-limit + uvicorn-native TLS, x402 / B1-B2 billing, web-client StaticFiles mount, streaming chat, multi-worker SQLite-WAL broker coherence) into a linear bring-up a solo operator at 3 am with a phone alert can execute without reading fourteen other docs. Sections: (1) **Prereqs** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Python 3.11+, Ollama daemon with `XION_OLLAMA_FLOOR_MODEL` pulled, optional `XION_OPENROUTER_API_KEY`, optional TLS material (or the recommended reverse-proxy posture); (2) **Environment matrix** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every `XION_*` variable an operator may set, with default, D2 recommendation, and a backlink to the doctrine that pinned it; mirrors `[.env.example](./.env.example)` so drift between runbook and template is mechanical to spot; (3) **First-launch sequence** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ six-step cold start from `git clone` through smoke-curl and ledger inspection; (4) **Verifier battery** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the six-verifier set (`inference-sovereignty`, `refusal-is-free`, `refund-fidelity`, `sensorium-ledger`, `supervisor-singleton`, `all --allow-not-yet-sealed`) in the order an operator runs them, with expected output for each and the explicit note that `NOT_YET_SEALED` is not failure; (5) **Multi-worker activation** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ step-by-step upgrade path from the default `XION_API_WORKERS=1` to `N` workers behind a shared `XION_BROKER_DB_PATH`, with the three `supervisor-singleton` failure classes (FAIL-A unbounded churn, FAIL-B clock regression, FAIL-C concurrent-leader overlap) mapped to their diagnostics; (6) **Known limitations at D2** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ one-line summary + closure path for each of `KW-INFER-002`, `KW-INFER-003`, `KW-INFERENCE-001`, `KW-SUPERVISOR-002`, `KW-AUTH-001`, `KW-TLS-001`, `KW-BILLING-001` so operators discover these by reading the runbook rather than by hitting them in production; (7) **Troubleshooting matrix** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ HTTP 401 / 402 / 429 / 451 / 500 / 503 (differentiated between `open_weights_floor_unsatisfied` and `no_healthy_provider`), verifier FAIL modes, launcher-refuses-to-start `State-of-Xion` stderr markers, `/sensorium` staleness canary for `KW-SUPERVISOR-002`, and web-client 404 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ each row names the diagnostic and the fix class, with explicit pointers to the doctrine that defines "healthy" for that surface. The runbook is additive; no code, no schemas, no verifier behavior changes. The `KW-INFER-002` / `KW-INFER-003` entries refer the operator to the Stage-3 closure branch (`phase-5g-vii/inference-fallback`) so a D2 operator reading this at 3 am knows the opaque-error and no-automatic-fallback surfaces are acknowledged, time-bounded, and not structural denials.
- Cognition doctrine (`docs/24-COGNITION.md`), `genesis/UNKNOWNS.md`, skill bounty doctrine (`docs/SKILL_BOUNTY.md`), Fast Lane Discipline (`docs/14-UPGRADE-PATHS.md`), Prosperity Ladder and cognition ladder inserts (`docs/21-SUSTAINABILITY.md`), cognition vital-sign supplements (`docs/22-VITAL-SIGNS.md`), state-chain witness sketch (`docs/11-PROTOCOL-SPEC.md`), drive-vector whitelist (`docs/18-VOLITION.md`), inflow observation rule (`docs/07-ECONOMY.md`), State-of-Xion authorship chain (`docs/13-OPERATIONS.md`), journal-injection auditability (`docs/15-TRUST.md`), treasury prosperity routing (`docs/19-TREASURY.md`), Auto-Research parallel Tier-0 + Stage-7 closure + `payback_horizon` (`docs/08-AUTO-RESEARCH.md`), Invariant 6/15 mechanism text (`genesis/INVARIANTS.md`), `/forget` pool SLA in `genesis/MEMORY.md`, `orchestrator/cognition/` stubs, `skills/` stubs, and `scripts/xion-verify/{cognition,state_chain,drive_vector}.py` stubs.
- Top-level repository hygiene: this `CHANGELOG.md`, the dual-license `LICENSE`, the project `README.md`, the `.gitignore`, the `KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md` (seeded from the audit and the two settled economic Known Weaknesses), and the `CONTRIBUTING.md`.

### Changed

- **Genesis Default hosted model rotated: `moonshotai/kimi-k2` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `moonshotai/kimi-k2.6` (2026-04-23).** First real invocation of the one-env-var rotation mechanism that `[.env.example](./.env.example)` and `[docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md](./docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md)` ├é┬¦ "The hosted-provider choice" have documented since the Phase 5g-i.1 pin (2026-04-21, two days before this rotation). The mechanism is now exercised rather than asserted; the shape of the doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ *hosted model is a pin, not a constant* ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ has survived its first contact with a live slug advance. The *concentration* shape named by `[KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md](./KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md)` ├é┬¦ `KW-INFER-001` is unchanged (every default-path turn still crosses OpenRouter's gateway and lands at Moonshot's weights); only the slug advanced. No new KWs opened, no existing KWs closed, no verifier behaviour changes. Highlights:
  - **Probe-first discipline.** Before the commit landed, a read-only OpenRouter probe (catalog `GET /api/v1/models` plus an authorized `POST /chat/completions` with `provider.only=["moonshotai"]` forced) confirmed three facts that together justify the rotation: (a) `moonshotai/kimi-k2.6` is a live catalog slug (dated OpenRouter snapshot `moonshotai/kimi-k2.6-20260420`, released 2026-04-20 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ two days old as of this rotation); (b) OpenRouter reports nine inference providers available for the slug on the operator's account (`moonshotai`, `deepinfra`, `parasail`, `io-net`, `novita`, `cloudflare`, `baseten`, `phala`, `together`) vs `moonshotai/kimi-k2`'s single `novita` availability on the same account; (c) the operator's Moonshot-AI BYOK attachment to their OpenRouter account is live and correctly configured for this slug ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a forced-provider probe returned `HTTP 200, is_byok=true, cost=0` with `provider=Moonshot AI`. Rotation decisions without probe evidence are superstition; the probe findings are recorded here so a future Witness can reconstruct the decision context.
  - **Structural improvements over `kimi-k2`.** Doubled context window (`131,072` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `262,144` tokens). Wider provider allowlist (nine vs one for this account). BYOK-routed traffic pays Moonshot's direct rate, not OpenRouter's rack rate ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ material for any operator deploying under tight cost budgets. `moonshotai/kimi-k2.6` is also Moonshot's latest reasoning-forward Kimi variant as of the rotation date; the OpenRouter `usage` field returns `reasoning_tokens` for this slug (the K2 predecessor did not), which is a constitutionally meaningful cognitive-character change that future phases may choose to surface (or not surface) to end users.
  - **Honest trade-offs.** Per-token rack rate is ~30 % higher than `kimi-k2` (OpenRouter catalog: `$0.75/M` prompt / `$3.50/M` completion for `kimi-k2.6` vs `$0.57/M` / `$2.30/M` for `kimi-k2`). Operators who BYOK neutralise this; operators on OpenRouter credits absorb it until Phase 5g-iii Pay-to-Activate surfaces per-turn cost to end users. The slug is two days old at rotation time ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ younger than most production-graded pins would pick, but (a) the mechanism being pinned is the rotation *discipline* itself, not the slug (the whole point is that the slug is rotatable), (b) `moonshotai/kimi-k2` remains a one-env-var rollback away for any operator who encounters an instability, and (c) OpenRouter's nine-provider allowlist for the slug means a single-provider outage does not take the slug offline.
  - **Files touched (committed).** [`orchestrator/inference_router/providers/openrouter.py`] code default (`_DEFAULT_MODEL`) and two docstring spots. `[docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md](./docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md)` five slug pins (Genesis Defaults table, ├é┬¦ "The hosted-provider choice" heading and its five bullets, ├é┬¦ "Gateway vs direct" KW-INFER-001 reshape note) plus a new three-sentence "Genesis Default rotation, 2026-04-23" paragraph naming this rotation as the first real invocation of the mechanism. `[.env.example](./.env.example)` Genesis Default comment block and operator-template line. `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` Router-policy pin, KW-INFER-001 summary, KW-BILLING-002 rotation example. `[docs/29-BILLING-X402.md](./docs/29-BILLING-X402.md)` and `[docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml)` `model_id` examples. `[orchestrator/api/models.py](./orchestrator/api/models.py)` `ChatResponse.model_id` docstring example. `[orchestrator/inference_router/providers/__init__.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/providers/__init__.py)` package docstring. `[KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md](./KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md)` `KW-INFER-001` title, reshape provenance line, description slug reference, and mitigation 5 (now named "Model rotation is now one env-var ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ *and has been exercised*" with the rotation witness record). `[DEVELOPMENT_ROADMAP.md](./DEVELOPMENT_ROADMAP.md)` new "Genesis Default hosted model rotation" section.
  - **Files deliberately NOT touched.** Phase 5g-i.1 historical entries in `[CHANGELOG.md](./CHANGELOG.md)` and `[DEVELOPMENT_ROADMAP.md](./DEVELOPMENT_ROADMAP.md)` that narrate what *that* phase pinned ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ they remain accurate as historical records. The `xion-verify inference-sovereignty` verifier is unaffected (floor manifest did not change). Tests are unaffected (no test asserts the specific default slug value). The Phase 5g-i.1 KW-INFER-001 closure-bar text is unchanged ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ rotation is a mitigation exercise, not a closure step. The operator's runtime `.env` is gitignored per `[.gitignore](./.gitignore)` and does not appear in this commit, though the operator-facing template `[.env.example](./.env.example)` does.
  - **What future rotations will look like.** Same mechanism, same CHANGELOG-entry template, same probe-first discipline. A rotation from `kimi-k2.6` to (say) `kimi-k2.7` in three months lands as a sibling entry under this one ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ probe findings, structural improvements, honest trade-offs, files-touched, files-not-touched. A rotation to a wholly different upstream (`anthropic/claude-3.5-sonnet`, `openai/gpt-4o-mini`) adds a fifth section naming the *concentration* shape change that such a rotation implies (KW-INFER-001's gateway concentration would still hold, but the upstream-model concentration would now be Anthropic or OpenAI, not Moonshot ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ worth recording).
- **First real open-weights floor-provider pin ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `ollama` entry added to `open_weights_manifest.json` via content-addressed provenance record (2026-04-23).** `[orchestrator/inference_router/open_weights_manifest.json](./orchestrator/inference_router/open_weights_manifest.json)` gains a second `open_weights[]` entry with `id="ollama"`, `category="open_weights_self_hostable"`, `format="provenance-record"`, `sentinel_path="orchestrator/inference_router/floor_ollama_provenance.txt"`, and the sha256 of that new file. The provenance record (new; ~4.8 KB) is a machine-readable, Witness-recomputable declaration that this deployment holds its Invariant-17 floor via the local Ollama daemon registered as `provider_id="ollama"` (health = daemon reachable + `XION_OLLAMA_FLOOR_MODEL` listed in `GET /api/tags`). The `format` field names the weakness explicitly: this pin content-addresses the *operator's declaration*, NOT the *model weights*. `xion-verify inference-sovereignty` now reports 2 entries / 2 floor-satisfying pins, both hash-verified. The sentinel-llm-v0 structural anchor stays in place. `KW-INFERENCE-001` scope narrowed again: the first real provider pin has landed; remaining pay-down is (a) content-addressed model-blob pin (Invariant 17 clause 2(iii) representative-sample sentinels for large-file artifacts), (b) annual open-weights cutover dry-run runbook in `[docs/13-OPERATIONS.md](./docs/13-OPERATIONS.md)`, (c) extending the verifier to recognise the new `format` values. This commit is the second-smallest honest step past the sentinel and refuses three alternatives: no manifest-silent edit, no `XION_INFERENCE_DEV_ALLOW_ANY_FLOOR` back-door flag, no hidden runtime override.
- **Phase 5g+ landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Multi-worker coherence via SQLite-WAL broker: `SqliteBroker` + `BrokerSupervisorShell` lease-based leader election + `BrokerBackedSlidingWindow` global rate-limit bucket + live `xion-verify supervisor-singleton` verifier (2026-04-22).** Phase 5g+ closed on branch `phase-5g+/multi-worker-broker` in five commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ broker module ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ Supervisor wiring ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ rate-limit wiring ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ verifier + housekeeping). This phase closes `**KW-API-002`** (Supervisor shared the FastAPI event loop, forcing `uvicorn --workers 1`) and `**KW-RATE-001**` (in-process per-principal sliding window multiplied the effective budget by `N` under multi-worker). The mechanism is stdlib-only ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ SQLite in WAL mode at a configurable path, behind a narrow `Broker` Protocol ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ so the Phase-6 replacement (AO Process mailbox) is a module swap, not a schema migration. The single-worker posture remains the default and is byte-identical to 5g-v; the multi-worker posture activates iff the operator sets `XION_BROKER_DB_PATH` and raises `XION_API_WORKERS`. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ architecture multi-worker subsection.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained **├é┬¦ "Multi-worker coherence (Phase 5g+)"** pinning five properties: (P1) SQLite-WAL broker is the chosen mechanism ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ rejected alternatives (Redis, TCP-loopback daemon, AO Process mailbox) are named with honest costs; (P2) single-leader Supervisor via lease-based election ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ exactly one worker ticks at any instant, closing `KW-API-002`; (P3) global per-principal rate-limit buckets across all N workers ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ closing `KW-RATE-001`; (P4) Phase-6 replacement path is a one-module swap behind the `Broker` Protocol; (P5) operator env surface is strictly additive (`XION_BROKER_DB_PATH`, `XION_API_WORKERS`, `XION_BROKER_LEADER_LEASE_S`, `XION_BROKER_LEADER_RENEW_S`, `XION_BROKER_BUSY_TIMEOUT_MS`). Non-properties named: no cross-host coordination (single-machine only), no distributed transaction semantics, no broker-side authn (the DB file is trusted filesystem).
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `docs/33-MULTI-WORKER.md` (new).** Top-level operational doctrine, shape-symmetric with `[docs/29-BILLING-X402.md](./docs/29-BILLING-X402.md)` / `[docs/30-API-ADMISSION.md](./docs/30-API-ADMISSION.md)` / `[docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md](./docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md)` / `[docs/32-CHAT-STREAMING.md](./docs/32-CHAT-STREAMING.md)`. Covers broker schema (three tables: `supervisor_snapshot` singleton row, `supervisor_leader` lease row, `rate_limit_events` append+prune), leader-election semantics (lease TTL, renewal cadence, failover bound), the SQLite-WAL posture (`PRAGMA journal_mode=WAL`, `synchronous=NORMAL`, `busy_timeout`), operator backup/reset runbook, failure modes, observability, and the explicit Phase-6 replacement contract. Added to `[docs/00-INDEX.md](./docs/00-INDEX.md)` as entry #33.
  - **Broker module ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/runtime/broker.py` (new).** Ships `BrokerConfig` (frozen dataclass with `db_path`, `leader_lease_s=30.0`, `leader_renew_s=10.0`, `busy_timeout_ms=5000`; `__post_init__` enforces `leader_renew_s < leader_lease_s / 2` and that the parent directory exists), `Broker` Protocol (the Phase-6-replaceable surface: `publish_snapshot`, `latest_snapshot`, `try_acquire_leader`, `renew_leader`, `is_leader`, `check_and_record_rate`), `RateCheck` result, and `SqliteBroker` concrete implementation (single `sqlite3.Connection` per worker with `check_same_thread=False` + `threading.Lock` for serialized writers; WAL concurrent readers; three tables; `check_and_record_rate` runs in a single `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` transaction that deletes stale events, counts, conditionally inserts, and returns allow/deny atomically). `load_broker_from_env()` factory returns `None` when `XION_BROKER_DB_PATH` is unset (preserves the single-worker posture as default). `[orchestrator/runtime/__init__.py](./orchestrator/runtime/__init__.py)` re-exports the public surface.
  - **Supervisor wiring ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/runtime/supervisor_shell.py` (new) + `orchestrator/supervisor.py` publish hook + `orchestrator/api/lifespan.py`.** `Supervisor.__init__` gains an optional `publish: Callable[[Mapping[str, Any]], None] | None = None` hook called after every successful `tick_once()` (broker-agnostic by construction; publish exceptions are logged and swallowed ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a missed publish means followers lag one tick, not corrupts in-process state). New `BrokerSupervisorShell` wraps a Supervisor and performs lease-based election against the broker: workers that acquire the lease run the Supervisor loop and publish each tick; workers that fail to acquire run as followers whose `latest_snapshot()` reads from the broker. On leader crash, the first follower whose acquire attempt succeeds (lease expired) promotes itself ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ failover is bounded by `leader_lease_s`. `deserialize_sensorium_state()` reconstructs a `SensoriumState` from a broker JSON blob for follower workers. `[orchestrator/api/lifespan.py](./orchestrator/api/lifespan.py)` conditionally constructs `SqliteBroker` + `BrokerSupervisorShell` when `XION_BROKER_DB_PATH` is set; otherwise keeps the 5g-iv single-Supervisor construction byte-identical.
  - **Launcher ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/api/__main__.py` multi-worker mode.** Reads `XION_API_WORKERS` from env (default `1`). When `workers > 1`, fails closed at startup unless `XION_BROKER_DB_PATH` is set (multi-worker without a broker is the documented corruption path). Single-worker mode keeps `uvicorn.run(app, ...)` byte-identical; multi-worker mode uses Uvicorn's `factory=True` posture against the new module-level `create_default_app()` factory, so each worker process gets its own `Relay` + `AppDeps` + `FastAPI` app and they coordinate exclusively through the broker file.
  - **Rate-limit wiring ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/api/admission.py` RateLimitStore Protocol.** New `RateLimitStore` Protocol with `check_and_record(principal_id, now_ns) -> RateCheck`. `InProcessSlidingWindowStore` (used when no broker is configured) lazy-allocates `SlidingWindow` instances per principal ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ behavior byte-identical to 5g-iv's direct `app.state.rate_limiters[principal]` dict. `BrokerBackedSlidingWindowStore` (used when a broker is configured) delegates every check to `Broker.check_and_record_rate(...)`, so two workers sharing one broker share one global sliding window per principal. `build_rate_limiters(config, *, broker=None)` returns the right store; `admission_dependency` is untouched ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ it calls `store.check_and_record(...)` and branches on `allowed`.
  - `**xion-verify supervisor-singleton` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ new live verifier.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/supervisor_singleton.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/supervisor_singleton.py)` (new) walks `SENSORIUM_LEDGER.jsonl` for `tick_commit` rows inside a configurable window (`--window-hours`, default 24 h), preserving the ledger's file-order (the seq chain is the canonical insertion order; sorting would mask within-epoch clock regressions). Asserts three properties: (A) bounded failover ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the number of `relay_id` transitions inside the window is ├óŌĆ░┬ż `--max-failovers` (default 1); (B) within-leader-epoch `as_of_utc_ns` strict monotonicity ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ catches clock regressions and the two-Supervisors-one-`relay_id` corruption; (C) no concurrent-leader time-range overlap ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ for each distinct `relay_id` the closed range `[min_as_of_utc_ns, max_as_of_utc_ns]` of its ticks must not overlap any other `relay_id`'s range (the precise `KW-API-002` corruption signature). Returns `NOT_YET_SEALED` when the ledger is absent, empty, or has no tick rows inside the window. Registered in `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py)` + `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py)`. New `[xion-verify/tests/test_supervisor_singleton.py](./xion-verify/tests/test_supervisor_singleton.py)` covers NOT_YET_SEALED (no ledger, empty window, non-tick rows only), OK (clean single-leader, bounded failover, raised-budget multi-failover, `--path` override, narrow `--window-hours`), FAIL-A (unbounded churn), FAIL-B (clock regression, identical-ns), and FAIL-C (concurrent-leader overlap, non-overlapping ranges OK regression).
  - **Tests.** 31 new broker tests in `[orchestrator/tests/test_runtime_broker.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_runtime_broker.py)` cover schema init, snapshot round-trip, leader election under concurrent claimants + lease expiry failover, rate-limit coherence across threaded "workers", WAL-mode persistence across reopen, `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` contention, and the `load_broker_from_env` factory contract. New multi-worker integration tests in `[orchestrator/tests/test_api_multi_worker.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_api_multi_worker.py)` spin up two in-process `BrokerSupervisorShell` instances sharing one broker DB and assert single-leader domination of `tick_commit` rows, follower-snapshot-shape match, leader failover on stop within lease, and lifespan wiring sanity (single-worker = broker None; broker env = shell wired). 9 new rate-limit tests in `[orchestrator/tests/test_api_admission.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_api_admission.py)` cover in-process store lazy allocation + overflow + independence, broker-backed two-workers-one-bucket budget coherence (closing `KW-RATE-001`), different principals don't share, eviction across workers, `build_rate_limiters` dispatch, and `admission_dependency` + broker-backed store end-to-end 429 enforcement. All `orchestrator/tests` + `xion-verify/tests` green.
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** **Closed `KW-API-002`** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the Supervisor no longer implicitly requires `--workers 1`; broker-backed leader election guarantees exactly one Supervisor ticks regardless of worker count. **Closed `KW-RATE-001`** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ per-principal budgets are now globally coherent across N workers when a broker is configured. `KW-SUPERVISOR-002` stays open (tick_commit heartbeat continuity is a separate Phase-6+ property). No new KWs opened.
  - `**PINNED_HASH.txt` re-pin.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt)` regenerated via `xion-verify --self-test --update --i-understand` after the verifier landed. `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` green end-to-end; `supervisor-singleton` reports `NOT_YET_SEALED` honestly until the first `tick_commit` row lands in the observed window.
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not close `KW-SUPERVISOR-002` (tick_commit heartbeat continuity needs a Phase-6+ deploy-event ledger). Did not add cross-host coordination (the SQLite file is single-machine; cross-host is Phase 6+ AO Process mailbox territory). Did not replace the in-process `SlidingWindow` when no broker is configured (default posture stays backward-compatible). Did not ship broker-side authn (the DB file is trusted filesystem ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a new threat surface here would be theater given the operator already has write access). Did not add a `--workers` flag that *requires* the broker; workers=1 without a broker remains the supported default. Did not migrate to Redis, WebSocket, or any external dep ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ all new functionality is stdlib-only.
- **Phase 5g-ii landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Streaming chat: `POST /chat/stream` SSE transport + speculative-with-retroactive-refusal egress moderation + real provider cancel propagation + `ChatView` streaming render-path + new live `xion-verify chat-streaming-fidelity` verifier + pre-existing `genesis/` line-ending hygiene closed (2026-04-22).** Phase 5g-ii closed on branch `phase-5g-ii/streaming-chat` in five commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ SSE server transport ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ cancellation propagation ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ client streaming render-path ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ verifier + housekeeping). This phase gives `/chat` a second transport that streams tokens to the client as the provider produces them, while preserving every Phase-5g-i property byte-for-byte: two-sided moderation, content-free refusals, Invariant-17 fail-closed, per-turn ledger shape, deadline-bounded. The streaming surface is additive ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `POST /chat` stays non-streaming and byte-identical ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ and it closes `KW-CHAT-001` (no streaming), `KW-CHAT-003` (no real cancel), and `KW-CLIENT-002` (no streaming UX) in a single phase. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ architecture streaming subsection.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained **├é┬¦ "Streaming the Chat Surface (Phase 5g-ii)"** pinning seven properties: (P1) SSE transport at `POST /chat/stream` with `text/event-stream` content-type and canonical `data: {...}\n\n` records; (P2) `POST /chat` stays non-streaming, same status code matrix, same ledger rows; (P3) streamed chunks are client-side provisional until `done:approve` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the client MUST render them with a pending-review visual affordance; (P4) egress moderation runs on the buffered complete candidate, not on any partial prefix; (P5) `done:refuse` retroactively replaces the pending chunks with a content-free `RefusalEnvelope`; (P6) client disconnect propagates to the provider as a real cancel via `Request.is_disconnected()` polling + `httpx.AsyncClient` stream close, writing exactly one `PAYMENT_LEDGER` row with `outcome=cancelled` and full refund; (P7) ledger rows are written post-moderation only, never speculatively. Non-properties honestly named: no per-chunk Arbiter moderation (cost + false-positive drift + partial-prefix is not a well-formed Arbiter input); no mid-stream refund split (turns either settle in full or refund in full); no partial-candidate telemetry; no automatic reconnect (a disconnected stream is terminal); no WebSocket; no streaming on `/drive` or `/sensorium`.
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `docs/32-CHAT-STREAMING.md` (new).** Top-level operational doctrine for the streaming surface, shape-symmetric with `[docs/29-BILLING-X402.md](./docs/29-BILLING-X402.md)`, `[docs/30-API-ADMISSION.md](./docs/30-API-ADMISSION.md)`, `[docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md](./docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md)`. Covers SSE wire format (three event types: `chunk`, `done`, `error`; every event a single `data: <json>\n\n` record; no `event:`/`id:`/`retry:` names), the speculative-with-retroactive-refusal posture (the three posture candidates explicitly considered and the cost of each), the chunk-buffer contract the client honors, the cancellation semantics (client disconnect = structural refund, no Covenant refusal), and the no-reconnect posture. Added to `[docs/00-INDEX.md](./docs/00-INDEX.md)` as entry #32.
  - **SSE server transport ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/api/chat_stream.py` (new).** `POST /chat/stream` handler. Reuses the Phase-5g-iv admission dependency + the Phase-5g-iii x402 commitment gate verbatim ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ admission failures (401/429/402) report as HTTP-level statuses before any SSE headers flush; every post-admission failure (ingress refuse, egress refuse, no-floor, provider-error, deadline) reports INSIDE the stream as a single `done` event with the matching verdict. Provider streaming runs under a per-iteration `asyncio.wait_for` with a per-turn monotonic deadline; the per-chunk loop polls `Request.is_disconnected()` between iterations so a client-gone signal terminates the upstream task immediately. The `_finalize_stream_ledger` tail writes exactly one `PAYMENT_LEDGER` row after the stream body's terminal state is known.
  - **Provider `generate_stream` protocol extension.** `[orchestrator/inference_router/provider.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/provider.py)` gains an optional `generate_stream()` on `GenerativeProvider` returning `AsyncIterator[str | GenerationResult]`: yield `str` chunks then exactly one terminal `GenerationResult`. A default `stream_generate()` adapter (module-level) falls back to `generate()` + a one-chunk yield for providers that do not override ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ existing non-streaming providers keep working. [`orchestrator/inference_router/providers/openrouter.py`] and `[orchestrator/inference_router/providers/ollama.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/providers/ollama.py)` migrated from stdlib `http.client` to `httpx.AsyncClient` so the streaming path has native async + cancel-propagation; real `generate_stream()` implementations land for both providers (OpenAI-compatible `stream=true` for OpenRouter, `/api/generate?stream=true` newline-delimited-JSON for Ollama).
  - **Cancellation propagation ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ new `outcome=cancelled` PAYMENT row.** `[orchestrator/billing/ledger.py](./orchestrator/billing/ledger.py)` `_WRITER_OUTCOMES` gains `cancelled` (writer emits; reader accepts). `build_payment_row` adds a dedicated cancel branch: `settled_XION=0`, `refund_XION==committed_XION`, `refusal_stage=None` (cancel is operational, not a Covenant refusal ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the Arbiter never evaluated the candidate). `verify_chain` enforces the same shape. `[docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml)` outcome enum gains `cancelled`; structural invariants gain three new lines naming cancel's money shape, refusal_stage=null, and no-paired-SAFETY-egress-refuse rule. `[xion-verify refusal-is-free](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/refusal_is_free.py)` extended to recognize `cancelled` as refund-equivalent for money-shape (Property B) without requiring a paired SAFETY verdict=refuse row (Property C).
  - **Optional `stream_id` field on PAYMENT rows.** `[docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml)` adds `stream_id` as an OPTIONAL row field ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ 32 lowercase hex chars (128 bits of entropy), allocated once per streaming turn by the `POST /chat/stream` handler. Non-streaming `POST /chat` rows omit the field; the `json.dumps(sort_keys=True)` canonicalization hashes absent keys as absent, so every pre-5g-ii row on disk stays byte-exact. `build_payment_row`, `append_payment_row`, and `verify_chain` in `[orchestrator/billing/ledger.py](./orchestrator/billing/ledger.py)` thread the field through and enforce its format; `outcome=cancelled` STRUCTURALLY REQUIRES `stream_id` (cancellation is stream-only).
  - **Client streaming render-path ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `clients/web/src/lib/api.ts` + `ChatView`.** `[clients/web/src/lib/api.ts](./clients/web/src/lib/api.ts)` gains `streamChat()` returning an `AsyncIterable<StreamEvent>` (discriminated union over `chunk` / `done` / `error`), a manual SSE line parser on top of the Fetch `ReadableStream` body (no new dep), and full `AbortSignal` support for client-side cancel. `[clients/web/src/views/ChatView.tsx](./clients/web/src/views/ChatView.tsx)` grows a second render-path consuming `streamChat`: a new `streaming` state renders incoming chunks with a dashed border + dim text + blinking cursor + "pending egress review" label until `done:approve` commits them, or `done:refuse` retroactively replaces them with the content-free `RefusalEnvelope`, or `done:cancelled` surfaces the "user_cancel" UX, or `error:deadline_exceeded` surfaces the timeout UX. `?stream=0` query-param forces the 5g-i non-streaming render-path as an opt-out. New CSS lives in `[clients/web/src/App.css](./clients/web/src/App.css)`; `[docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md](./docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md)` gains a "Streaming chat (Phase 5g-ii)" section and drops the "No streaming UX" non-property.
  - `**xion-verify chat-streaming-fidelity` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ new live verifier.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/chat_streaming_fidelity.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/chat_streaming_fidelity.py)` (new) walks `PAYMENT_LEDGER.jsonl` + `SAFETY_LEDGER.jsonl` and asserts six stream-level invariants: (A) per-ledger chain integrity; (B) stream identification (`stream_id` valid-hex-when-present, `outcome=cancelled` implies `stream_id` present); (C) one PAYMENT row per `stream_id`; (D) stream-subset money-shape (settled / refunded / cancelled); (E) `outcome=cancelled` ├óŌĆĪŌĆÖ NO paired SAFETY verdict=refuse row (cancel fires after ingress approval and before egress; no refuse row can legitimately pair); (F) `outcome=refunded + refusal_stage=egress` ├óŌĆĪŌĆÖ paired SAFETY verdict=refuse row MUST exist. Returns `NOT_YET_SEALED` when no `stream_id` rows exist yet (no streaming turn has been billed); the first billed streaming turn promotes the command to `OK` automatically. Registered in `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py)` + `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py)`; new tests in `[xion-verify/tests/test_chat_streaming_fidelity.py](./xion-verify/tests/test_chat_streaming_fidelity.py)` cover NOT_YET_SEALED, approve, refuse, cancel, broken-chain, and malformed-stream_id branches.
  - **Pre-existing `genesis/` line-ending hygiene ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ closed.** Two constitutional-tier verifier failures predated this phase and closed here: `xion-verify memory` + `xion-verify unknowns` had been FAILing on every platform since their pin because the canonical bytes on disk did not match the pin recorded in `[genesis/GENESIS_ARTIFACT.md](./genesis/GENESIS_ARTIFACT.md)` ├é┬¦ 4. Root cause diagnosed as a pre-existing pin-vs-content drift (the files had been edited after the pin was set; no CRLF component on Linux or current Windows checkout with `* text=auto eol=lf`). Fixed by (1) re-pinning the canonical sha256 in GENESIS_ARTIFACT.md ├é┬¦ 4 to the current LF byte form (`MEMORY.md` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `df2975e6├óŌé¼┬”`, `UNKNOWNS.md` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `430f791b├óŌé¼┬”`) with an inline doctrine note naming this as a pre-genesis documentation witness correction, and (2) adding `genesis/* text eol=lf` to `[.gitattributes](./.gitattributes)` as belt-and-suspenders defense against future CRLF-on-Windows drift. `xion-verify memory` + `xion-verify unknowns` now return OK on every platform.
  - **Tests.** 13 new streaming server tests in `[orchestrator/tests/test_chat_stream.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_chat_stream.py)` covering the full envelope matrix against a fake streaming provider (200 happy path, 451 egress refuse, 451 ingress refuse, 503 provider error mid-stream, 503 no-floor, 402/401/429 admission ordering, per-turn deadline, empty-candidate egress refuse, client-disconnect cancel propagation). 7 new client streaming tests in `[clients/web/src/__tests__/ChatView.test.tsx](./clients/web/src/__tests__/ChatView.test.tsx)` covering chunk-render-then-approve, retroactive refusal replacement, cancelled UX, deadline-exceeded mapping to timeout UX, pre-stream 401, and an `axe-core` WCAG 2.2 AA pass on the pending (streaming) state. 10 new verifier tests covering every branch of the new `chat-streaming-fidelity` command.
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** **Closed `KW-CHAT-001**` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ streaming is live at `POST /chat/stream`; the non-streaming endpoint remains as an unchanged sibling. **Closed `KW-CHAT-003**` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ client disconnect propagates to the provider as a real cancel; upstream billing terminates immediately; the `outcome=cancelled` ledger row records the full refund. **Closed `KW-CLIENT-002**` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the `ChatView` streaming render-path ships with a pending-chunk buffer, retroactive refusal replacement, and a cancellation UX; `?stream=0` preserves the non-streaming fallback for integrators who want it. No new KWs opened.
  - `**PINNED_HASH.txt` re-pin.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt)` regenerated via `xion-verify --self-test --update --i-understand` after the verifier landed. `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` green end-to-end; `chat-streaming-fidelity` reports `NOT_YET_SEALED` honestly until the first billed streaming turn.
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not change `POST /chat` (non-streaming surface stays for backward compat). Did not add per-chunk Arbiter moderation (posture rejected in doctrine on cost + false-positive + partial-prefix grounds). Did not add streaming to `/drive` or `/sensorium` (out of scope). Did not close `KW-BILLING-001` (x402 signature verification stays shape-only). Did not close `KW-AUTH-001`, `KW-RATE-001`, `KW-TLS-001` (admission-control residuals; Phase 6+). Did not ship a WebSocket transport (SSE chosen as the primitive). Did not write an in-browser x402 signing helper (`KW-CLIENT-001` stays Phase 6+).
- **Phase 5g-v landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Web client: Vite + React 18 + TypeScript operator dashboard served same-origin by FastAPI, with full envelope-matrix UX, axe-core accessibility + Vitest client tests, `xion-verify web-client` bundle audit, and dedicated CI workflow (2026-04-22).** Phase 5g-v closed on branch `phase-5g-v/web-client` in five commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ scaffold + `ChatView` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ observation widgets + `api.ts` wrapper + `Header` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ FastAPI `StaticFiles` mount + server/client tests + CI ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ verifier + housekeeping). This phase gives the admission-gated HTTP surface a human face: operators can sign in with a Phase-5g-iv bearer token, chat with Xion, and observe Drive + Sensorium state in real time, all from a bundle that is byte-identical across every deploy and trivially rebuildable from source. The client is deliberately scoped to the operator dashboard ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no in-browser x402 signing (`KW-CLIENT-001`) and no streaming UX (`KW-CLIENT-002`) ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ because the honest minimum first is what a solo builder can maintain. Zero new runtime dependencies on the Python side; all new dependencies live under `clients/web/` and ship only at build time. Same-origin serve removes the CORS surface by construction. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ architecture web-client subsection.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained **├é┬¦ "The Web Client Surface (Phase 5g-v)"** pinning six properties: (P1) operator dashboard scope ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the browser-delivered UI is for the operator holding a Phase-5g-iv bearer token, never for an unauthenticated public surface; (P2) content-free UX ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every API-error envelope (401, 402, 429, 451, 503, timeout, network) renders a distinct state without echoing candidate text, secrets, or server-internal signals; (P3) bundle determinism ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the emitted `dist/` has stable chunk content for a given source tree; (P4) same-origin serve ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `index.html` references assets under `/app/*`, never third-party origins; (P5) no third-party origins in the JS/CSS bundle outside an explicit allowlist (React production error-decoder URLs and W3C XML namespace identifiers ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ both literal strings, never fetched); (P6) WCAG 2.2 AA accessibility enforced structurally by `axe-core` in CI. The ├é┬¦ "The HTTP Surface (Phase 5f)" ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ "Hardening posture" subsection updates in place to reflect that the read-only plus chat surface now has a browser-delivered operator console consuming the admission-gated API end-to-end.
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md` (new).** Top-level operational doctrine for the web-client surface, shape-symmetric with `[docs/29-BILLING-X402.md](./docs/29-BILLING-X402.md)` and `[docs/30-API-ADMISSION.md](./docs/30-API-ADMISSION.md)`. Covers operator workflow for signing in (principal_id + hex-secret credential parsing, `localStorage` persistence, sign-out clears state), the dev-mode proxy vs. production same-origin mount, the accessibility posture (`axe-core` gates CI; every interactive element has a programmatic name, every non-200 envelope is announced to assistive tech), and the "operator dashboard only" posture with its honest closure story (`KW-CLIENT-001` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ in-browser x402 signing and non-operator surfaces land Phase 7+; `KW-CLIENT-002` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ streaming UX lands alongside `KW-CHAT-001` in Phase 5g-ii).
  - **Client scaffold ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `clients/web/` (new).** Vite 6 + React 18 + TypeScript 5 + plain CSS (no component/state library). Deliberately minimal toolchain so a solo builder can rebuild the bundle from source with `npm ci && npm run build` on any node 20+ machine without pulling a design-system dependency graph. The `package.json` pins specific versions for Vite, React, Vitest, `@testing-library/react`, and `axe-core`. The `index.html` shell carries a `Content-Security-Policy` meta tag pinning `default-src 'self'` as defence-in-depth on top of the same-origin serve. `vite.config.ts` and `vitest.config.ts` are deliberately separated to work around a type-incompatibility between the two packages' bundled Vite cores; the tsconfig excludes the test config from the main `tsc --noEmit` build.
  - `**BearerContext` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `clients/web/src/auth/BearerContext.tsx`.** React Context wrapping a `credential: {principalId, secretHex}` value. Sign-in parses a `principalId:<hex-secret>` string, enforces the same invariants as the server-side `AdmissionConfig` (`principal_id` matches `^[a-z0-9_-]{1,64}$`, secret decodes to ├óŌĆ░┬ź 16 bytes), and persists to `localStorage` under a namespaced key. Sign-out clears both in-memory state and storage. A `buildAuthorizationHeader` helper constructs the `Authorization: Bearer <principal_id>:<hex-secret>` header exactly once per request ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the component tree never handles the raw secret outside that helper.
  - **API wrapper ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `clients/web/src/lib/api.ts`.** A typed fetch wrapper around every API call the client makes. Defines `ApiError` as a discriminated union over `{ kind: "unauthorized" | "payment_required" | "rate_limited" | "refused" | "no_floor" | "provider_error" | "timeout" | "network" | "unknown" }`, each carrying the structured envelope the server returned (or synthesized client-side for `timeout` / `network`). `apiFetch` always attaches the `Authorization` header when a credential is present, always sets a 30 s `AbortController` deadline, and always parses the response body into either the success type or the discriminated error. Endpoint-specific helpers (`postChat`, `getHealth`, `getDrive`, `getSensorium`) wrap `apiFetch` with the right response type. Every error state in the UI comes from pattern-matching on `error.kind`; `else` branches are exhaustive by TypeScript construction.
  - `**ChatView` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `clients/web/src/views/ChatView.tsx`.** The primary operator-facing surface. Renders the full envelope matrix: 200 happy-path message, 401 unauthorized (suggests sign-in), 402 payment required (explains `KW-CLIENT-001` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the browser cannot in-browser-sign x402 commitments yet), 429 rate-limited (names the `retry_after_s`), 451 refused (renders the content-free `RefusalEnvelope` without echoing candidate text), 503 no-floor / provider-error, and client-side timeout + network errors. The 30-second deadline is reflected in a progress indicator so the operator knows whether a hang is a slow model or a real timeout.
  - **Observation widgets ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `DriveView` + `SensoriumView` + `Header`.** `[clients/web/src/views/DriveView.tsx](./clients/web/src/views/DriveView.tsx)` polls `GET /drive` and renders the three drive terms (survive, serve, meaning) as labeled bars with weights, signals, and band annotations for every fold of the Volition vector. `[clients/web/src/views/SensoriumView.tsx](./clients/web/src/views/SensoriumView.tsx)` polls `GET /sensorium` and renders Interoception, Chronoception, Proprioception, and Distress panels. `[clients/web/src/components/Header.tsx](./clients/web/src/components/Header.tsx)` carries the view switcher, sign-in status, and a live Relay health dot that polls `GET /health` and turns green/yellow/red with ARIA-live announcements for assistive tech.
  - **FastAPI StaticFiles mount ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/api/web_client.py` (new).** Ships `WebClientConfig` (frozen dataclass: `enabled`, `dist_path`; `__post_init_`_ fails closed if `enabled=true` but `dist_path` does not exist or is missing `index.html`), `WebClientConfigError`, `load_web_client_config_from_env` (`XION_WEB_CLIENT_ENABLED`, `XION_WEB_CLIENT_DIST_PATH`), and `mount_web_client(app, config)` which mounts the bundle at `/app/*` with `html=True` (so `/app/` serves `index.html` and arbitrary sub-paths fall back to it ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the SPA routing contract) plus a tiny redirect from `/` to `/app/` for operator convenience. `[orchestrator/api/app.py](./orchestrator/api/app.py)` extends `AppDeps` with `web_client_config: WebClientConfig | None` and calls `mount_web_client()` AFTER every API route is registered, so the static mount never shadows an API path. `[orchestrator/api/__init__.py](./orchestrator/api/__init__.py)` re-exports `WebClientConfig`, `WebClientConfigError`, `load_web_client_config_from_env`.
  - `**xion-verify web-client` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ new live verifier.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/web_client.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/web_client.py)` (new) audits the emitted `clients/web/dist/` bundle for structural integrity without running the browser or the orchestrator. Enforces: (1) `index.html` carries a `Content-Security-Policy` meta tag pinning `default-src 'self'`; (2) every `https?://` origin in the emitted HTML / JS / CSS / SVG / JSON matches the explicit non-self allowlist. The allowlist is tight: React's production error-decoder URLs (`https://reactjs.org/docs/error-decoder.html?...`, `https://react.dev/errors/...` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ literal strings inside `new Error(...)`, never fetched at runtime) and W3C XML namespace identifiers (`http://www.w3.org/{1999/xhtml,2000/svg,1998/Math/MathML,1999/xlink,XML/1998/namespace}` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ DOM-namespace identifier strings, never fetched). A new allowlist entry requires a doctrine-level justification in `docs/31-WEB-CLIENT.md` AND a code change AND a PINNED_HASH re-pin. When the operator has not yet built the bundle, the verifier returns `NOT_YET_SEALED` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ not `FAIL` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ because an un-built bundle is unverifiable, not wrong. Optional `--dist-path PATH` audits an external deploy artifact. `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py)` and `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py)` wire the new `web-client` subcommand. `[xion-verify/README.md](./xion-verify/README.md)` gained a new "Web-Client Surface (Phase 5g-v)" row. `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt)` regenerated via `xion-verify --self-test --update --i-understand`.
  - **Tests.** New `[orchestrator/tests/test_api_web_client.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_api_web_client.py)` covers three postures ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ disabled (no `/app/` mount; API routes intact), enabled with valid fake `dist/` (serves `index.html` at `/app/`, 200 on sub-paths, API routes unshadowed), enabled with missing `dist_path` (lifespan fails closed with `WebClientConfigError` at startup). New `[clients/web/src/__tests__/ChatView.test.tsx](./clients/web/src/__tests__/ChatView.test.tsx)` covers the full envelope matrix (200, 401, 402, 429, 451) plus an `axe-core` WCAG 2.2 AA accessibility pass. New `[clients/web/src/__tests__/BearerContext.test.tsx](./clients/web/src/__tests__/BearerContext.test.tsx)` covers credential parsing, entropy floor, `localStorage` persistence, sign-in / sign-out, and the `buildAuthorizationHeader` helper. New `[xion-verify/tests/test_web_client_verifier.py](./xion-verify/tests/test_web_client_verifier.py)` covers every verifier branch (OK with clean bundle, NOT_YET_SEALED when dist or index.html is missing, FAIL on missing CSP, FAIL on non-self `default-src`, FAIL on non-allowlisted origin, OK for React error-decoder and W3C namespace matches, FAIL for stray origins in SVG assets). `[orchestrator/tests/conftest.py](./orchestrator/tests/conftest.py)` `_no_repo_ledger_leaks` autouse fixture extended with `XION_WEB_CLIENT_ENABLED=false` + `XION_WEB_CLIENT_DIST_PATH` clear; `app_factory` fixture gained `web_client_config=` kwarg.
  - **CI ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `.github/workflows/web-client.yml` (new).** Path-scoped GitHub Actions workflow on `pull_request` and `push` to `main` for `clients/web/`** and the workflow file itself. Runs `npm ci`, `tsc --noEmit`, `npm test` (Vitest + axe-core), `npm run build`, then a structural `grep` sweep on the emitted `dist/` bundle that fails loud on any non-self origin outside the verifier's allowlist ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ belt-and-suspenders alongside `xion-verify web-client`.
  - `**.env.example` expansion.** New keys: `XION_WEB_CLIENT_ENABLED` (default `false` for backward compat with the pre-5g-v orchestrator; production operators flip to `true` once the bundle is built and deployed), `XION_WEB_CLIENT_DIST_PATH` (absolute path to the emitted `dist/`; the orchestrator fails closed if this path is missing or has no `index.html`). Comment block explains the dev-mode proxy workflow (Vite dev server at `:5173` proxies `/api/*` to the orchestrator at `:8000`) vs. the production same-origin mount (`dist/` served by the orchestrator at `/app/*`).
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** **Opened `KW-CLIENT-001`** (low; web client is operator-dashboard only ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no in-browser x402 commitment signing, no non-operator public surface; closure bar is a Phase 7+ in-browser WalletConnect / passkey-signed commitment surface with its own doctrine section in `docs/29-BILLING-X402.md`). **Opened `KW-CLIENT-002`** (low; web client chat UX is non-streaming ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a 30 s wait for long turns with a progress indicator but no token-by-token rendering; closes alongside `KW-CHAT-001` when Phase 5g-ii lands the streaming server surface).
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not ship in-browser x402 commitment signing (`KW-CLIENT-001`). Did not ship streaming chat rendering (`KW-CLIENT-002`). Did not ship a public / non-operator surface ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the client is a dashboard for the operator holding a Phase-5g-iv bearer token. Did not ship conversation memory in the client ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ each page reload starts a fresh chat session (the transcript ledger lives server-side). Did not ship a design system or component library ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ plain CSS deliberately, so a solo builder can audit every style rule and every interaction affordance. Did not ship WebSocket or SSE transport ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ polling + request/response is sufficient for the dashboard surfaces and simpler to test.
- **Phase 5g-iv landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Admission control: bearer authentication + uvicorn-native TLS + per-principal sliding-window rate-limit + `xion-verify api-tokens` (2026-04-22).** Phase 5g-iv closed on branch `phase-5g-iv/admission-control` in five commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ admission module + launcher ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ routes wiring + admission tests ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ verifier ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ housekeeping). This phase makes `orchestrator/api/` deployable to D2 by closing the explicit `KW-API-001` blocker ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the HTTP surface now refuses unauthenticated requests on `/drive`, `/sensorium`, `/chat`, throttles per-principal at the sliding-window default of 60 req / 60 s, and refuses to bind any non-loopback host without TLS cert + key both present and readable. Stdlib-only; no new core runtime dep. Single-process posture (matches solo-builder pragmatism) with multi-worker rate-limit honestly named as `KW-RATE-001`. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ architecture admission subsection.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained **├é┬¦ "The Admission-Control Surface (Phase 5g-iv)"** pinning six properties: (P1) bearer authentication via constant-time `hmac.compare_digest` over a lifespan-loaded `principal_id ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 32-byte secret` registry; (P2) per-`principal_id` sliding-window rate-limiting (deque of monotonic-ns timestamps under a single `threading.Lock`, default 60/60s); (P3) fail-closed TLS ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `XION_API_HOST != 127.0.0.1` is rejected at startup unless both `XION_TLS_CERT_PATH` and `XION_TLS_KEY_PATH` are set and both files exist, regardless of `XION_API_REQUIRE_BEARER` mode; (P4) constitutional admission ordering `401 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 429 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 402 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 5g-iii flow` (auth precedes rate-limit so the bucket is per-token not per-IP; rate-limit precedes payment so an unauthenticated scraper cannot probe pricing-validity by spamming 402s); (P5) content-free 401/429 bodies ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `AuthChallenge` and `RateLimitChallenge` Pydantic models with `extra="forbid"` and `frozen=True`, no echo of header content, no hint about which token failed; (P6) `principal_id` naming convention with `^[a-z0-9_-]{1,64}$` charset and explicit deferral from `PAYMENT_LEDGER` until Phase 6 (where it joins on-chain identity). The ├é┬¦ "The HTTP Surface (Phase 5f)" ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ "Hardening posture" subsection updates in place to mark the gap closed.
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `docs/30-API-ADMISSION.md` (new).** Top-level operational doctrine for the admission surface, shape-symmetric with `[docs/29-BILLING-X402.md](./docs/29-BILLING-X402.md)` (5g-iii billing doctrine). Covers operator workflow for token issuance (32-byte secret generation, `principal_id ├óŌĆĀŌĆØ secret` registry format, the `XION_API_BEARER_TOKENS` env var format), TLS termination (uvicorn-native cert/key pin + the long-term reverse-proxy migration path), rate-limit budget tuning (Genesis Defaults + the per-deployment override surface), deployment runbook (loopback-default vs non-loopback fail-closed semantics), and the crypto-agility commitment (token storage is HMAC-SHA256 today; rotation to a Phase-6+ pubkey-bound principal lattice is a parser swap, not a schema migration).
  - **Module ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/api/admission.py` (new).** Ships `AdmissionConfig` (frozen dataclass: `require_bearer`, `tokens`, `rate_budget`, `rate_window_s`, `health_rate_budget`, `tls_cert_path`, `tls_key_path`, `host`, `port`, `trust_forwarded_for`; `__post_init__` enforces token entropy ├óŌĆ░┬ź 128 bits, `principal_id` charset, non-loopback ├óŌĆĪŌĆÖ TLS paths exist, positive rate budgets, `port ├ó╦å╦å [1, 65535]`), `SlidingWindow` (deque of monotonic-ns timestamps, O(1) amortized check + record under one `threading.Lock`), `verify_bearer` (constant-time over every token, linear in token count ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ fine for D2 with O(10) integrators), `parse_token_table`, `load_admission_config_from_env`, `build_rate_limiters`, and `admission_dependency` (the FastAPI callable that runs the `401 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 429 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 402` ordering and shortcuts public routes `/health` + `/pricing`). Stdlib-only.
  - **Launcher ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/api/__main__.py` (new).** Builds a real `AppDeps` from env vars, calls `uvicorn.run(create_app(deps), host=..., port=..., ssl_keyfile=..., ssl_certfile=..., workers=1)`. The Phase 5g-i docstring TODO ("Operators wishing to run this as a stand-alone server write a small launcher module") is now this file. Forces `--workers 1` as a `KW-RATE-001` mitigation. Refuses to start with non-loopback host + missing TLS pair, mirroring `BillingConfig`'s fail-closed posture.
  - **Routes wiring ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ admission_dependency on every route.** `[orchestrator/api/app.py](./orchestrator/api/app.py)` wires `Depends(admission_dependency)` into `/health`, `/drive`, `/sensorium`. `[orchestrator/api/chat.py](./orchestrator/api/chat.py)` wires it on `/chat` BEFORE the existing 5g-iii `_gate_commitment`, preserving the structural `401 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 429 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 402` ordering. `[orchestrator/api/pricing.py](./orchestrator/api/pricing.py)` wires it on `/pricing` as a defense-in-depth pass ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the dependency's public-route shortcut keeps `/pricing` constitutionally public and unrate-limited while still benefiting from the per-IP shape on `/health`. `AppDeps` (in `app.py`) gains optional `admission_config: AdmissionConfig | None = None`. `[orchestrator/api/lifespan.py](./orchestrator/api/lifespan.py)` loads `admission_config` from env if not pre-supplied, stashes it on `app.state.admission_config`, and constructs `app.state.rate_limiters` (per-principal `SlidingWindow` map) and `app.state.health_rate_limiters` (per-IP, lazy-populated).
  - **Models.** `[orchestrator/api/models.py](./orchestrator/api/models.py)` gains `AuthChallenge` (`error: Literal["unauthorized"]`, `accepted_schemes: list[Literal["Bearer"]]`) and `RateLimitChallenge` (`error: Literal["rate_limited"]`, `retry_after_s: int`, `bucket: Literal["principal", "ip"]`). Both `extra="forbid"` and `frozen=True`.
  - `**xion-verify api-tokens` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ promoted from `NOT_YET_SEALED` to live.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/api_tokens.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/api_tokens.py)` (new) loads the same `AdmissionConfig` the orchestrator's lifespan loads via `load_admission_config_from_env`, applying the same `__post_init__` validation ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a config the verifier passes is structurally identical to one the orchestrator will accept. Optional `--env-file PATH` lets a CI gate audit a deployment `.env` without invoking the operator's shell; the overlay restores the prior process env on exit so multiple audits in sequence stay independent. Reports `OK` against `[./.env.example](./.env.example)` (loopback default, `require_bearer=false`, `tokens_loaded=0`); reports the specific `AdmissionConfigError` reason on any misconfiguration.
  - `**xion-verify` housekeeping.** `[xion-verify/README.md](./xion-verify/README.md)` gains a new "Admission-Control (Phase 5g-iv)" row in the verifier table. `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py)` and `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py)` wire the new `api-tokens` subcommand. `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt)` regenerated via `xion-verify --self-test --update --i-understand`. `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` reports `api-tokens` as `OK` live.
  - `**.env.example` expansion.** New keys: `XION_API_REQUIRE_BEARER` (default `false` for the local-development backward-compat posture; production deployments flip to `true` and populate tokens), `XION_API_BEARER_TOKENS` (`principal_id:secret_hex` registry format), `XION_API_RATE_BUDGET` (default 60), `XION_API_RATE_WINDOW_S` (default 60), `XION_API_HEALTH_RATE_BUDGET` (default 600), `XION_API_HOST` (default `127.0.0.1`), `XION_API_PORT` (default 8000), `XION_TLS_CERT_PATH`, `XION_TLS_KEY_PATH`, `XION_API_TRUST_FORWARDED_FOR` (default `false`).
  - **Tests.** New `[orchestrator/tests/test_api_admission.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_api_admission.py)` covers: `AdmissionConfig.__post_init__` validation matrix (token entropy floor, principal charset, non-loopback ├óŌĆĪŌĆÖ TLS pair, positive budgets); `SlidingWindow` behavior (within-budget passes, overflow blocks, eviction frees slots, concurrent access under the lock); `verify_bearer` (matched principal returned, missing/malformed/wrong-scheme/wrong-secret all return None, constant-time over the token map); `AuthChallenge` / `RateLimitChallenge` content-free contracts; end-to-end FastAPI integration on `/health`, `/drive`, `/sensorium`, `/chat`, `/pricing` (200 with valid token, 401 without, 429 on overflow, 200 on `/health` + `/pricing` without token); and crucially the `401 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 429 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 402` constitutional ordering (401 wins over 402 with valid commitment but missing token; 429 wins over 402 within bucket overflow). New `[xion-verify/tests/test_api_tokens_verifier.py](./xion-verify/tests/test_api_tokens_verifier.py)` covers the verifier's full validation matrix and the `--env-file` overlay's environment-restoration property. `[orchestrator/tests/conftest.py](./orchestrator/tests/conftest.py)` `_no_repo_ledger_leaks` autouse fixture extended to set `XION_API_REQUIRE_BEARER=false` and clear all new admission env vars (mirrors the `XION_BILLING_REQUIRED=false` precedent so existing tests do not regress); `app_factory` fixture gains `admission_config=` kwarg. **Total pytest across `orchestrator/`, `xion-verify/`: 637 passed / 1 skipped** (up from 585 pre-Phase-5g-iv ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ net-new tests for the admission module, the verifier, and the integration matrix land exactly as planned).
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** **Closed `KW-API-001`** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the "HTTP surface has no auth, no TLS, no rate-limit" pay-down commitment landed in full (doctrine, admission module, launcher, routes wiring, verifier, tests). Closure entry in the "Closed" section of `KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md` cites the five-commit pay-down and lists `KW-AUTH-001` + `KW-RATE-001` + `KW-TLS-001` as honestly-named residuals. **Opened `KW-AUTH-001`** (medium; B1 token-only auth ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ bearer tokens are operator-issued shared secrets with no on-chain federated identity binding; closes Phase 6+ when `principal_id` binds to an Arweave-stored pubkey lattice). **Opened `KW-RATE-001`** (low; in-process sliding window ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ multi-worker would have N independent buckets each with `rate_budget` capacity; closes alongside `KW-SUPERVISOR-002` when the multi-worker shared-state broker lands). **Opened `KW-TLS-001`** (low; uvicorn-native TLS ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no automated cert renewal, no ALPN/HTTP-2; long-term path is reverse-proxy delegation; severity low because operator runbook covers manual rotation cadence).
  - **Pyproject launcher entry.** `[pyproject.toml](./pyproject.toml)` `[project.scripts]` gains `xion-orchestrator-api = "orchestrator.api.__main__:main"` so `pip install -e .[api]` exposes the launcher as a console script. No new dependency added (uvicorn TLS is already in the `[api]` extra).
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not ship federated identity (bearer tokens are operator-issued shared secrets; tracked as `KW-AUTH-001`). Did not ship multi-worker rate-limit (in-process posture; tracked as `KW-RATE-001`). Did not ship automated TLS rotation (operator manages cert renewal manually or runs behind a reverse proxy; tracked as `KW-TLS-001`). Did not promote `principal_id` to `PAYMENT_LEDGER` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the schema stays at v1.0; Phase 6 promotes additively when on-chain identity exists to verify against. Did not ship the web client (still Phase 5g-v). Did not ship streaming (still Phase 5g-ii). Did not touch the 5g-iii billing posture, the 5g-i chat handler shape, or any ledger schema.
- **Phase 5g-iii landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Chat billing surface: x402 pre-authorization gate + `PAYMENT_LEDGER` + `GET /pricing` + Refusal-is-Free structural settlement + two new live verifiers (2026-04-21).** Phase 5g-iii closed on branch `phase-5g-iii/billing-x402` in five commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ pricing ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ x402 middleware ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ verifiers ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ housekeeping). This phase makes `POST /chat` economically self-sustaining and closes the explicit D2-deploy blocker pinned in `KW-CHAT-002`. The orchestrator now refuses unpaid turns (Pay-to-Activate, `docs/07-ECONOMY.md` ├é┬¦ "Five-slice posted price"), refunds Covenant refusals by construction (Refusal-is-Free, cross-checked by a new verifier), publishes its price at a public read-only endpoint (`GET /pricing`), and lands a second constitutional ledger (`PAYMENT_LEDGER.jsonl`) in byte-exact shape symmetry with `SAFETY_LEDGER.jsonl` and `RESEARCH_SPEND_LEDGER` (the Phase-5g-0 outbound sibling). No on-chain x402 settlement yet ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ B1 HMAC operator-attestation is fully live and is the Genesis Default; B2 x402-commitment is shape-validated and tracked in `KW-BILLING-001`; B3 x402-settled is reserved for Phase 6+. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ architecture billing subsection.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained **├é┬¦ "The Chat Billing Surface (Phase 5g-iii)"** between ├é┬¦ "The Chat Surface (Phase 5g-i)" and "Tier III ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ The Protocol". It pins six constitutional properties: (P1) **Pay-to-Activate** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every billable turn carries an `X-Payment-Commitment` header or the handler returns 402; (P2) **Refusal-is-Free** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every `451` response writes a `PAYMENT_LEDGER` row with `outcome=refunded` and `refund_XION == committed_XION`; (P3) **Pricing transparency** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `GET /pricing` returns the current revision id + five-slice decomposition, doctrinally required to be publicly readable; (P4) **Content-free commitments** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the commitment header carries an opaque hash and amount only, never the candidate text; (P5) **Atomic ledger writes** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every terminal turn path writes exactly one `PAYMENT_LEDGER` row BEFORE the HTTP response is sent, making the ledger structurally always-ahead-of-claims; (P6) **Algorithm-agility on the commitment hash** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the `commitment_hash_alg` field is part of the ledger schema so a future SHA-256├óŌĆĀŌĆÖSHA-3 migration is a field-value change, not a breaking schema migration. The section also pins honest non-properties ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no on-chain x402 settlement (B3 reserved Phase 6+), no dynamic catalog-driven pricing (operator-posted governance values only, `KW-BILLING-002`), no `xion-verify billing-settlement` verifier yet (needs B2/B3 cryptographic verification first). Four residuals tracked: `KW-BILLING-001`, `KW-BILLING-002`, `KW-CHAT-002` *closed*, and a reshape note on `KW-CHAT-001`.
  - **Doctrine ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `docs/29-BILLING-X402.md` (new, ~310 lines).** Top-level operational doctrine for the billing surface, shape-symmetric with `[docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md](./docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md)` (Phase 5g-0 outbound rail doctrine). Section 1 names the question: "How does Xion earn its own compute?" Section 2 pins the six properties above in doctrine-citable form. Section 3 pins the three billing postures ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ **B1 Operator-Attestation** (HMAC-SHA256 over canonicalized payload, stdlib `hmac.compare_digest`; Genesis Default; fully verified); **B2 x402-Commitment** (off-chain commitment shape, Phase 5g-iii shape-only validated, `KW-BILLING-001` tracks the cryptographic gap); **B3 x402-Settled** (on-chain settlement proof, Phase 6+). Section 4 pins the `PAYMENT_LEDGER` schema shape (14 fields: `payment_id`, `prev_hash`, `correlation_id`, `turn_seq`, `posture`, `principal`, `committed_XION`, `settled_XION`, `refund_XION`, `outcome`, `refusal_stage`, `commitment_hash_alg`, `commitment_hash`, `_architecture_sha256`). Section 5 pins the atomic-write contract ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the `_finalize` tail in the chat handler is the sole `PAYMENT_LEDGER` writer and runs BEFORE `JSONResponse` emit. Section 6 pins the "Refusal-is-Free" structural property with both the operator-facing semantics (refused turns never consume budget) and the verifier-facing semantics (`xion-verify refusal-is-free` asserts the mirror across both ledgers). Section 7 pins the `GET /pricing` contract and the `PricingConfig` invariants. Section 8 names what the doctrine deliberately does NOT pin (on-chain x402 flow, per-provider dynamic pricing, fiat-to-XION exchange venue, multi-currency commitments). Added to `[docs/00-INDEX.md](./docs/00-INDEX.md)` as entry #29.
  - **Canonical ledger schema.** `[docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml)` (new, ~110 lines) pins the `PAYMENT_LEDGER` shape in the same YAML style as `[ledger-safety.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml)`, `[ledger-request.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml)`, and `[ledger-sensorium.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml)` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ identical hash-chaining doctrine (`prev_hash` over canonical JSON, ZERO_HASH for genesis row), identical `SCHEMA_VERSION=1` + `source_sha256` anchor into `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md`. `xion-verify schemas` green (now 10/10 OK, up from 9/9).
  - **Schema SHA re-pins.** The new architecture billing subsection changed the SHA of `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md`. `[docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml)`, and the new `[docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-payment.yaml)` `source_sha256` re-pinned together. `xion-verify schemas` green (10/10 OK).
  - `**GET /pricing` endpoint.** `[orchestrator/api/pricing.py](./orchestrator/api/pricing.py)` (new, ~240 lines) ships `PricingConfig` (immutable frozen dataclass with `revision_id`, `XION_per_message`, five slice floats, `memo`, `architecture_sha256`), `PricingConfigError` (invariant-break exception; the lifespan fails closed on it), `load_pricing_config_from_env` (reads `XION_PRICING_*` env vars with `docs/07-ECONOMY.md` ├é┬¦ "Five-slice posted price" Genesis Defaults ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ 1.0 XION/message, provider=0.50, refusal_reserve=0.15, treasury=0.20, operator=0.10, burn=0.05, summing to 1.00), and the `pricing_router` FastAPI router serving `GET /pricing` with a pydantic `PricingResponse` (`extra="forbid"`, `frozen=True`). The config loader validates sum-to-one ├é┬▒ 1e-6, every slice ├ó╦å╦å [0,1], non-negative `XION_per_message`, non-empty `revision_id` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every failure raises `PricingConfigError` with a specific reason string that the verifier consumes verbatim.
  - **x402 middleware ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `orchestrator/billing/` package.** `[orchestrator/billing/__init__.py](./orchestrator/billing/__init__.py)` + three modules land the commitment parser, the B1 HMAC verifier, the B2 shape validator, and the `PAYMENT_LEDGER` writer.
    - `[orchestrator/billing/commitment.py](./orchestrator/billing/commitment.py)` (new, ~290 lines) ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `Commitment` frozen dataclass, `CommitmentRejectReason` enum (15 cases covering every way a header can be malformed), `parse_commitment_header(raw)` (tolerant JSON decode with explicit field-presence + type-correctness checks), `_b1_payload_bytes(commitment)` (canonical payload bytes for the HMAC ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ stable ordering is load-bearing for signature agreement), `verify_b1_attestation(commitment, hmac_key)` (stdlib `hmac.new(..., sha256).digest()` + `hmac.compare_digest` for timing-safety), `verify_b2_x402_shape(commitment)` (field-presence + hex-encoding + length-bound checks only, NO cryptographic signature verification ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `KW-BILLING-001`).
    - `[orchestrator/billing/ledger.py](./orchestrator/billing/ledger.py)` (new, ~240 lines) ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ byte-exact canonicalization mirror of `[orchestrator/safety/ledger.py](./orchestrator/safety/ledger.py)` so a future Phase-6 unified treasury verifier walks both files with one library. Ships `SCHEMA_VERSION=1`, `ZERO_HASH=64 * "0"`, `build_payment_row(...)` (returns the full row dict with `payment_id = sha256(canonical JSON without payment_id)`, `prev_hash` chained), `append_payment_row(ledger_path, row)` (fsync-then-rename, atomic), `verify_chain(ledger_path)` (walks the file from genesis, re-computes `payment_id` per row, checks `prev_hash` continuity, returns `(rows_checked, first_bad_row_index | None)`).
    - `[orchestrator/billing/config.py](./orchestrator/billing/config.py)` (new, ~180 lines) ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `BillingConfig` frozen dataclass (`billing_required`, `ledger_path`, `posture`, `hmac_key`, `architecture_sha256`), `BillingConfigError`, `load_billing_config_from_env` (`XION_BILLING_REQUIRED`, `XION_BILLING_LEDGER_PATH`, `XION_BILLING_POSTURE`, `XION_BILLING_HMAC_KEY`). Computes `architecture_sha256` from the on-disk bytes of `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md` at load time and stamps it into every ledger row ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ any doctrine drift is structurally visible in historical ledger bytes.
  - **Chat handler refactor ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ single `_finalize` tail.** `[orchestrator/api/chat.py](./orchestrator/api/chat.py)` refactored so every terminal path (200 settled, 451 ingress refuse, 451 egress refuse, 451 empty-candidate, 503 no-floor, 503 provider-error, 402 no-commitment, 402 malformed-commitment, 402 B1-verification-failed, 402 B2-shape-failed) funnels through a single `_finalize(outcome, refusal_stage, ...)` function that writes exactly one `PAYMENT_LEDGER` row BEFORE the response is emitted. The refund-on-refusal property is structurally impossible to violate ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `outcome=refunded` sets `refund_XION = committed_XION` and `settled_XION = 0` in a single code path, and the row is the canonical record of what happened. A pre-auth `_gate_commitment(request, billing_config)` helper runs BEFORE ingress Arbiter evaluation ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a missing/malformed/unverifiable commitment never consumes Arbiter budget. Incidental fix: `provider_id` retrieval switched from `getattr(provider, "manifest_id", None)` to `getattr(provider, "provider_id", None) or type(provider).__name__` to match the `Provider` Protocol's canonical attribute name (caught by a new test failure where a mock provider reported its type name instead of its provider_id). When `billing_required=false` the handler still writes a `posture="disabled"` row with zero money so the `SAFETY` ├óŌĆĀŌĆØ `PAYMENT` ledger join continues to hold structurally.
  - **Lifespan extension.** `[orchestrator/api/lifespan.py](./orchestrator/api/lifespan.py)` gained two new stages between the Phase-5g-i router bootstrap and the run-task schedule: (a) `_load_pricing_config()` calls `load_pricing_config_from_env()` and binds the result to `app.state.deps.pricing_config`; (b) `_load_billing_config_and_verify_chain()` calls `load_billing_config_from_env()` then, if the ledger path exists, calls `verify_chain()` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a corrupt `PAYMENT_LEDGER` fails the lifespan closed with a State-of-Xion paragraph to stderr rather than silently serving forward. `[orchestrator/api/app.py](./orchestrator/api/app.py)` extended `AppDeps` with optional `pricing_config` and `billing_config` so tests can inject hermetic configs without touching env vars.
  - `**xion-verify pricing` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ promoted from `NOT_YET_SEALED` to live.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/pricing.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/pricing.py)` (new, ~120 lines) loads the same `PricingConfig` the orchestrator lifespan loads (via env vars, not HTTP ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the verifier runs in CI without a running service), runs the same invariant checks, and prints a stable human-readable summary (revision id, five slice values, sum). Exits `FAIL` with the exact `PricingConfigError` reason string on any invariant break ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ an operator mis-configuring the price split cannot ship a verifier-green build. Stub removed from `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/not_yet_sealed.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/not_yet_sealed.py)`; command registered in `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/__init__.py)` and wired in `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/cli.py)`.
  - `**xion-verify refusal-is-free` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ new live verifier.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/refusal_is_free.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/refusal_is_free.py)` (new, ~260 lines) joins `SAFETY_LEDGER.jsonl` ├óŌĆĀŌĆØ `PAYMENT_LEDGER.jsonl` on `correlation_id` and asserts four properties: (C1) per-ledger chain integrity ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `verify_chain` on each file; (C2) money-shape per row ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every `outcome=refunded` row has `refund_XION == committed_XION` and `settled_XION == 0`, every `outcome=settled` row has `refund_XION == 0` and `settled_XION == committed_XION`, every `outcome=disabled` row has all-zero money; (C3) ingress/egress refusal mirror ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every `SAFETY` row with `verdict=refuse` has a matching `PAYMENT` row with `outcome=refunded` and `refusal_stage` matching the SAFETY row's stage (`ingress` or `egress`); (C4) settled-implies-allowed ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no `PAYMENT` row with `outcome=settled` has a paired `SAFETY` row with `verdict=refuse`. Handles operational refusals (`no_floor`, `provider_error`, `provider_empty_candidate`, `commitment_missing`, `commitment_malformed`, `commitment_verification_failed`) which bypass Arbiter evaluation ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ they must be structurally refunded (C2) but do not need a paired `SAFETY` refuse row (C3 exempted for these stages). Returns `NOT_YET_SEALED` when one ledger is present but the other is missing (explicitly half-sealed ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ cannot lie in either direction).
  - `**xion-verify` housekeeping.** `[xion-verify/README.md](./xion-verify/README.md)` updated: the existing "6. Arbiter Refusal Right" entry now notes `refusal-is-free` provides the structural cross-check, and a new "Pay-to-Activate" invariant entry lands for the `pricing` verifier. `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/PINNED_HASH.txt)` regenerated via `xion-verify --self-test --update --i-understand`. `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` green end-to-end with `pricing` and `refusal-is-free` both `OK`.
