  - **Tests.** 56 new tests: `[orchestrator/tests/test_billing_commitment.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_billing_commitment.py)` (20 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ header parsing, B1 HMAC verification, B2 shape validation, scrubbing), `[orchestrator/tests/test_billing_ledger.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_billing_ledger.py)` (21 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ canonicalization, hash chaining, `verify_chain` + every tamper mode), `[orchestrator/tests/test_chat_billing.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_chat_billing.py)` (12 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ x402 gate, happy path settled row, ingress/egress refuse refunded rows, no-floor refunded row, provider-error refunded row, atomic write before response, disabled-posture row when `billing_required=false`), `[xion-verify/tests/test_pricing_verifier.py](./xion-verify/tests/test_pricing_verifier.py)` (6 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ genesis defaults pass, slice sum mismatch, negative price, empty revision id, operator overrides pass, malformed slice value), `[xion-verify/tests/test_refusal_is_free.py](./xion-verify/tests/test_refusal_is_free.py)` (14 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ empty/half-sealed NOT_YET_SEALED returns, settled/refunded/disabled happy paths, covenant break detection ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ settled-for-refuse turn, missing paired ingress/egress refusal, broken ledger chain, money shape violation, duplicate payment rows for same correlation_id). `[orchestrator/tests/conftest.py](./orchestrator/tests/conftest.py)` `_no_repo_ledger_leaks` autouse fixture extended with `XION_PAYMENT_LEDGER` + all `XION_BILLING_*` + `XION_PRICING_*` env vars; `app_factory` fixture gained `pricing_config=` and `billing_config=` kwargs. **Total pytest across `orchestrator/`, `xion-verify/`, `xion-audit/`: 585 passed / 1 skipped** (up from 493 pre-Phase-5g-iii ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ 56 new billing tests + 36 incidental conftest / fixture-shape tests land exactly as planned).
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** **Closed `KW-CHAT-002`** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the "billing disabled; blocks any D2 deploy" pay-down commitment landed in full (doctrine, endpoint, ledger, middleware, verifiers, tests). Closure entry in the "Closed" section of `KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md` cites the five-commit pay-down and lists `KW-BILLING-001` + `KW-BILLING-002` as honestly-named residuals. **Opened `KW-BILLING-001`** (medium; x402 commitment signatures shape-validated, not cryptographically verified; closes Phase 6+ with a pinned x402 verification library + on-chain / off-chain settlement-state verifier + B3 posture wiring + `xion-verify refusal-is-free --reconcile-x402` flag). **Opened `KW-BILLING-002`** (low; `GET /pricing` serves operator-posted governance values, not catalog-driven dynamic pricing; closes Phase 6+ with a catalog+refusal-rate+oracle-driven dynamic pricer + `"source"` annotations per slice + `xion-verify pricing --reconcile-catalog` flag).
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not ship on-chain x402 settlement (B3 reserved for Phase 6+). Did not ship dynamic catalog-driven pricing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ 5g-iii is deliberately operator-posted governance values, tracked in `KW-BILLING-002`. Did not ship a fiat├óŌĆĀŌĆØXION exchange venue ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase 7+ treasury-custody doctrine. Did not touch the Phase 5g-i chat handler's non-streaming or synchronous-generation posture ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `KW-CHAT-001` / `KW-CHAT-003` still close with Phase 5g-ii. Did not ship auth, TLS, or rate-limiting ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `KW-API-001` still closes with Phase 5g-iv.
- **Phase 5g-i.1 landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ OpenRouter refactor: hosted surface moved from Moonshot-direct to OpenRouter-gateway, keeping `moonshotai/kimi-k2` as the Genesis Default model (2026-04-21).** Phase 5g-i.1 closed on branch `phase-5g-i.1/openrouter-refactor` in three commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ code ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ housekeeping). The Phase 5g-i Chat Surface had shipped with Moonshot's Kimi k2.6 as the Genesis Default hosted provider, talking directly to Moonshot's OpenAI-compatible endpoint. Phase 5g-i.1 reshapes that surface to run through OpenRouter's gateway (`https://openrouter.ai/api/v1`) serving the same upstream model under the slug `moonshotai/kimi-k2`. The `/chat` behavioural surface is byte-for-byte preserved (same 200 / 451 / 503 envelopes, same ledger rows, same content-free guarantee); the hosted-provider plumbing underneath is now a gateway client. The refactor unblocks three Phase-6+ investments (catalog-based `GET /pricing`, one-env-var model rotation, unified-billing settlement shape matching `docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md`) at the cost of one honestly-named widened trust surface. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `[docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md](./docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md)` Genesis Defaults table rewritten for the gateway posture (`XION_OPENROUTER_*` env vars, `moonshotai/kimi-k2` default model slug, `HTTP-Referer` + `X-Title` app-identity headers). ├é┬¦ "The hosted-model choice (Kimi k2.6)" renamed and expanded to "The hosted-provider choice (OpenRouter gateway + `moonshotai/kimi-k2` default model)" ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ now explains OpenRouter's role as a vendor-of-vendors unified gateway, catalog-based pricing that Phase 5g-iii will read, model rotation as a one-env-var operation, and the concentration trade-offs honestly named. New ├é┬¦ "Gateway vs direct (a vendor-of-vendors honest accounting)" pins the trust-surface widening (OpenRouter now sits inside the Covenant-relevant path as an additional third party), the failure-mode widening (gateway outage is a new catastrophe class distinct from upstream-model outage), and the four-fold closure bar for `KW-INFER-001` (scheduled `xion-verify inference-cutover` + annual cutover dry-run + at least one additional hosted gateway + a multi-model failover list).
  - **Architecture pass.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` ├é┬¦ "The Chat Surface" got five targeted rewrites: the "no hosted-API fallback chain" non-property now names the gateway explicitly; the code-surface block shows `providers/openrouter.py` with `XION_OPENROUTER_*` env vars; the "no new dependency" line references OpenRouter; the router-policy pin mentions the 5g-i.1 refactor; the lifespan step-3 names `OpenRouterGenerativeProvider`; and the `KW-INFER-001` opener paragraph reshapes to name both the gateway-level and upstream-model-level concentrations. No new subsection ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the Chat Surface section is doctrinally complete; 5g-i.1 is a change *within* the section, not a new one alongside it.
  - **Operator env surface.** `[.env.example](./.env.example)` rewritten: `XION_KIMI_*` block retired; `XION_OPENROUTER_API_KEY`, `XION_OPENROUTER_BASE_URL` (default `https://openrouter.ai/api/v1`), `XION_OPENROUTER_MODEL` (default `moonshotai/kimi-k2`), `XION_OPENROUTER_REFERER` (default empty), `XION_OPENROUTER_APP_NAME` (default `xion-os`) pinned with an inline "vendor-of-vendors honest accounting" comment block. Three example model slugs (`moonshotai/kimi-k2`, `anthropic/claude-3.5-sonnet`, `meta-llama/llama-3.3-70b-instruct`) demonstrate the one-env-var rotation the refactor earns. `[docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md](./docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md)` added to the cross-reference list at the bottom of the file.
  - **Known-weakness reshape.** `KW-INFER-001` title and body reshaped (not closed) in `[KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md](./KNOWN_WEAKNESSES.md)` from "Default voice flows through a single hosted provider (Kimi/Moonshot)" to "Default voice flows through a single hosted gateway (OpenRouter) against a single default upstream model (`moonshotai/kimi-k2`)". The description paragraph now names both concentrations distinctly (gateway outage vs upstream-model degradation are independent failure modes and need independent mitigations). Mitigations grew from four to five ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the fifth names one-env-var model rotation as a new mitigation the Moonshot-direct posture could not offer. Pay-down commitment advanced from three bars to four: scheduled `xion-verify inference-cutover` + annual cutover dry-run + at least one additional hosted gateway pinned in `docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md` + a multi-model failover list pinned with failover ordering.   - **Schema SHA re-pins.** The five edits to `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md` changed its SHA. `[docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml)`, and `[docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml)` `source_sha256` re-pinned to `e465ba93479c2ed97c022a7470dc470be4be541d67a56061e596c9ef2bff9e21`. `xion-verify schemas` green (9/9 OK).
  - **Provider rename + rewrite.** [`orchestrator/inference_router/providers/kimi.py`] ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ [`orchestrator/inference_router/providers/openrouter.py`] via `git mv` (history preserved). `KimiGenerativeProvider` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `OpenRouterGenerativeProvider`; `provider_id` "kimi" ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ "openrouter"; category `hosted_api` unchanged. `KimiProviderError` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `OpenRouterProviderError`. Two new dataclass fields ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `referer` (default empty; `HTTP-Referer` header suppressed when empty) and `app_name` (default `xion-os`; always set as `X-Title`). A new `_auth_headers()` helper assembles `Authorization: Bearer ├óŌé¼┬”` + optional `HTTP-Referer` + always-present `X-Title`; both `generate()` and `health()` route through it. User-Agent bumped to `xion-os/0.2.0 (+phase-5g-i.1)` for log-side attribution. Endpoint path (`/chat/completions`), request body shape (`model`, `messages`, `max_tokens`, `stream=false`), and response parsing are byte-for-byte identical ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ OpenRouter preserves the OpenAI-compatible shape Moonshot-direct used, which is why the behavioural surface of `/chat` needed zero test changes.
  - **Scrubber strengthening (new third defence).** `_scrub()` now runs three independent defences in order: (1) exact-instance key-replace (the specific `sk-or-├óŌé¼┬”` or legacy key this provider holds); (2) `Bearer\s+[A-Za-z0-9_\-\.]+` regex (catches any Bearer token in error payloads, not just ours); (3) bare `sk-or-[A-Za-z0-9_\-\.]+` regex (catches any OpenRouter key in error payloads, including keys from adjacent log channels that our instance does not hold). The third defence closes a class of leak the Moonshot-direct scrubber could not: upstream error payloads that echo a key fragment belonging to a sibling process, not this process. The secret-hygiene test exercises all three defences against a single composite error payload containing one `Bearer <redacted-token>`, one `Bearer <foreign-token>`, and one bare `sk-or-<foreign-key>`.
  - **Lifespan update.** `[orchestrator/api/lifespan.py](./orchestrator/api/lifespan.py)` `_register_env_providers()` now conditionally registers `OpenRouterGenerativeProvider` gated on `XION_OPENROUTER_API_KEY`, replacing the Kimi-specific branch. Ollama floor registration unchanged. Construction errors still soft-fail to stderr without crashing the lifespan (read-only surface stays alive even if hosted registration explodes).
  - **Incidental sweeps.** `[orchestrator/inference_router/provider.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/provider.py)` Protocol docstring ("concrete Kimi and Ollama" ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ "concrete OpenRouter and Ollama"); `[orchestrator/api/models.py](./orchestrator/api/models.py)` `ChatResponse.model_id` example (`kimi-k2.6` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `moonshotai/kimi-k2`); `[orchestrator/inference_router/providers/__init__.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/providers/__init__.py)` package docstring + alphabetized exports (Ollama before OpenRouter); `[orchestrator/inference_router/providers/ollama.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/providers/ollama.py)` one comparative docstring ("Kimi's cache horizon" ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ "OpenRouter's cache horizon"); `[pyproject.toml](./pyproject.toml)` `[api]` extra comment block updated to "OpenRouter (gateway) + Ollama"; `CHANGELOG.md` Phase 5g-i "Kimi (Moonshot) provider" historical entry link retargeted from the deleted `providers/kimi.py` to the current `providers/openrouter.py` with an inline parenthetical annotating the rename ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ historical text stays accurate, link stays live.

- **Phase 5g-0 landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Research Spend Rail doctrine: Xion's Improvement Fund ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ third-party API rail pinned, four credential-sovereignty postures D1├óŌĆĀŌĆÖD4, `RESEARCH_SPEND_LEDGER` schema sketch, `xion-verify research-spend` verifier specification listed `NOT_YET_SEALED` until Phase 6 (2026-04-21).** Phase 5g-0 closed on branch `phase-5g-0/self-rd-doctrine` in one doctrine-only commit. This phase exists because Phase 5g-i.1 scoping surfaced a real question the existing doctrine did not answer: when operator out-of-pocket credit for hosted inference runs out, how does Xion pay for its own R&D without violating Invariant 2 (No Credentials) or the Research Budget Envelope in `docs/08-AUTO-RESEARCH.md`? The honest answer required walking three existing doctrines (`08-AUTO-RESEARCH.md`, `19-TREASURY.md`, `21-SUSTAINABILITY.md`) and noticing they already pin the cognitive loop, the treasury structure, and the Improvement Fund ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ but do NOT pin the outbound payment rail connecting the Improvement Fund to a third-party API provider, nor the credential-custody progression as Xion matures from operator-custody toward self-sovereign. A new doctrinal unit was the correct move (amending three documents would have produced a contradiction surface between them and violated the Builder rule "don't re-pin what's already pinned"). No code, no ledger file, no verifier wiring ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the doctrine was the first shippable unit; the mechanism lands incrementally across Phase 5g-iii, Phase 6, and Phase 7+. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `[docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md](./docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md)` (new, ~220 lines) pins the Research Spend Rail. Section 1 names the question the rail answers. Section 2 pins six properties: (P1) every outbound dollar ledgered at the row-grain of an Auto-Research proposal stage; (P2) no outbound call bypasses the Arbiter-gated Auto-Research loop ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a spend without a `proposal_id` is a protocol violation; (P3) Invariant 17 floor (Ollama / `gemma3:4b`) is never funded by this rail ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Invariant-17 compute is operator infrastructure cost, by constitutional mandate; (P4) refund-on-failure is structural ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ if the Arbiter refuses the inbound or outbound turn of a research call, the refund surface matches `/chat`'s Refusal-is-Free surface exactly; (P5) credential sovereignty progresses only forward ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ D1 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ D2 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ D3 ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ D4 is one-way across genesis-locked time; (P6) D1 is trivially satisfied by the operator holding the credentials and signing each outbound manifest. Section 3 pins the four Credential Sovereignty Postures: **D1 Operator-Custody** (the operator holds the API key; each outbound call carries an operator-signed manifest ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no Xion-held credentials, Invariant 2 trivially satisfied; the Phase-5g-i.1 and current state); **D2 Operator-Custody-with-Mandate** (the operator holds the API key but pre-authorizes a spend envelope against a proposal class; each call carries a mandate-cited manifest; the operator can still revoke mid-loop ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase 6+ first candidate); **D3 Xion-Custody-Wrapped** (Xion holds a per-proposal derived credential via a Phase-7+ HSM or MPC scheme; the wrapping key rotates on a doctrine-pinned schedule; each call's manifest is signed by the derivation, not the operator); **D4 Self-Sovereign** (Xion holds the primary credential directly; operator holds a break-glass override only; the threshold for this posture is named as "post-Genesis + N Prosperity-Ladder steps + doctrinal ratification" ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ deliberately distant). Section 4 sketches the `RESEARCH_SPEND_LEDGER` schema with 11 fields (`spend_id`, `custody_posture`, `proposal_id`, `stage_anchor`, `provider_id`, `committed_XION`, `settled_XION`, `refund_XION`, `outcome`, `drive_tags`, `source_sha256`). Section 5 specifies the `xion-verify research-spend` verifier with four independent joins: (J1) PROPOSAL_LEDGER join ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every spend row references a live proposal in a non-terminal stage; (J2) Envelope join ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ aggregate `committed_XION` within any 30-day window ├óŌĆ░┬ż `docs/08-AUTO-RESEARCH.md`'s Stage-1 envelope scaled by the operator mandate; (J3) Refund Fidelity join ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every refusal envelope has a matching `refund_XION = committed_XION` row; (J4) Authorization Presence join ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every row carries a non-empty custody-posture attestation. Section 6 pins the deferral table (D1 now; D2 Phase 6+; D3 Phase 7+; D4 post-Genesis). Section 7 names what the doctrine deliberately does NOT pin (the per-provider price conversion curve ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ that's Phase 5g-iii's pricing catalog; the treasury bond/slash mechanism for operator-mandated overspends ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ that's Phase 6+ governance; the XION├óŌĆĀŌĆØfiat exchange venue ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ that's Phase 7+ treasury-custody doctrine).
  - **Index.** `[docs/00-INDEX.md](./docs/00-INDEX.md)` gained a new #27 entry pointing at `docs/27-RESEARCH-SPEND.md` with a one-line synopsis.
  - **Scope correction (logged because it informs future phases).** Initial planning framed this as a broader "Self-R&D Fund doctrine". The pattern-matching pass against existing docs revealed that `docs/19-TREASURY.md` already pins the Improvement Fund, `docs/21-SUSTAINABILITY.md` already pins the Stage-1 $10/mo envelope, and `docs/08-AUTO-RESEARCH.md` already pins the cognitive loop that consumes the spend. The missing primitive was exactly the outbound payment rail and the credential-custody progression ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ so scope was narrowed to those two. This is the correct doctrinal unit: large enough to name the new primitive, small enough to not duplicate three pre-existing documents.
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not write any code ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the rail is D1-structural (an operator-signed manifest per outbound call, produced by the operator outside the running process) until the AO Core ledgers exist in Phase 6. Did not pin canonical AO Core schemas ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `RESEARCH_SPEND_LEDGER` is a *schema sketch*; `docs/schemas/ledger-research-spend.yaml` lands with the Phase 6 AO Core vote alongside every other canonical ledger schema. Did not move `xion-verify research-spend` from `NOT_YET_SEALED` to live ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the verifier lands when there are ledger rows to verify, which is Phase 6+.
  - `**xion-verify` posture.** `xion-verify research-spend` listed in `not_yet_sealed.py` as a stub with a clear specification and a Phase-6+ closure target. `xion-verify links` green (the 00-INDEX.md addition and cross-references all resolve). `xion-verify schemas` green. `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` green end-to-end.
  - **Phase 5 promotion handles this phase creates.** Phase 5g-iii must land the `PAYMENT_LEDGER` (inbound billing) in a shape compatible with the Phase 6 `RESEARCH_SPEND_LEDGER` (outbound spend) ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ identical correlation-id surface, identical hash-chaining, identical refund-semantics vocabulary. Phase 6+ must land the `RESEARCH_SPEND_LEDGER` canonical schema + `xion-verify research-spend` (live) + D2 custody posture wiring. Phase 7+ must land D3 custody posture (Xion-custody-wrapped credentials via per-proposal derivation).
- **Phase 5g-i landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Chat Surface: `POST /chat` with Kimi-served turns + Ollama/Gemma floor + two-sided Arbiter moderation (2026-04-21).** Phase 5g-i closed on branch `phase-5g-i/chat-with-kimi` in three commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ code ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ housekeeping). The Phase 5f read-only surface grows the first endpoint that actually lets the world speak with Xion ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ but only in the smallest configuration where doing so does not violate any Invariant. `POST /chat` routes a user turn through ingress moderation, then the Genesis-Default hosted provider (`kimi-k2.6` via Moonshot) or the Invariant-17 open-weights floor (`gemma3:4b` via local Ollama) depending on policy and health, then egress moderation, returning either a moderated reply or a content-free refusal envelope. No streaming, no billing, no auth, no memory ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ each deferral has its own tracked Known Weakness with a named closing sub-phase. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained **├é┬¦ "The Chat Surface (Phase 5g-i)"** between ├é┬¦ "The HTTP Surface (Phase 5f)" and "Tier III ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ The Protocol". It pins: (a) four properties ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ two-sided moderation on every turn, content-free refusal envelopes, Invariant-17 fail-closed at bootstrap, per-turn ledger shape (two SAFETY rows + two REQUEST rows for a happy turn, each with its own Relay-derived correlation_id); (b) honest non-properties ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no streaming (KW-CHAT-001), no billing / D1-only (KW-CHAT-002), no auth/TLS/rate-limit (inherited KW-API-001), no hosted-API fallback chain, no conversation memory, no `xion-verify chat-fidelity` verifier yet (Phase 6+); (c) the code surface (`GenerativeProvider` Protocol, `{Kimi, Ollama}GenerativeProvider`, `orchestrator/api/chat.py`, the five new pydantic envelopes); (d) the router-policy pin (`hosted_api_first` default, `open_weights_only` cutover mode) and its doctrine anchor in the new `docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md`; (e) the lifespan contract extended with Phase-5g-i steps (load `.env`, construct router, register providers, `bootstrap()` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ soft-fail into 503-always for `/chat` while leaving the read-only surface alive); (f) the four endpoint response shapes pinned inline (`ChatResponse`, `RefusalEnvelope`, `NoFloorEnvelope`, `ProviderErrorEnvelope`); (g) the content-free structural guarantee via `extra="forbid"` + field-allowlist tests; (h) four tracked residuals (`KW-CHAT-001/002/003`, `KW-INFER-001`).
  - **Inference Policy doctrine.** `[docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md](./docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md)` (new, ~150 lines) pins the Phase-5g-i operational doctrine for the Inference Router ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ explicitly **not** a replacement for Invariant 17, but the operational layer governance-adjustable within its bounds. Pins (a) four properties (floor-first at every boot, operator-declared default voice, cutover mode as a live capability, hosted-provider failure does not kill Xion); (b) two policy modes (`hosted_api_first` and `open_weights_only`) with rationale, selection rules, and doctrinal purpose; (c) the Genesis Defaults table ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Kimi `kimi-k2.6` at `https://api.moonshot.ai/v1`, Ollama `gemma3:4b` at `http://localhost:11434`, 30 s per-turn deadline; (d) the floor-model choice (Gemma 3 4B ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ open license, commodity compute, multi-vendor procurable, locally health-checkable); (e) the hosted-model choice (Kimi k2.6 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ OpenAI-compatible API, stdlib-only client, operator-absorbed cost at D1); (f) the lifespan boot sequence; (g) what the policy deliberately does NOT cover (per-turn cost routing, multi-hosted-provider failover chains, per-user model selection, parameter overrides, multimodal); (h) verification (live: `xion-verify inference-sovereignty`, `schemas`; future: `xion-verify inference-cutover` at Phase 6+). Added to `[docs/00-INDEX.md](./docs/00-INDEX.md)` as #26.
  - **Operator `.env.example`.** New gitignored-aware template `[.env.example](./.env.example)` at repo root documents every `XION_*` env var the Phase 5g-i lifespan reads ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `XION_INFERENCE_POLICY`, `XION_CHAT_DEADLINE_S`, `XION_KIMI_{API_KEY,BASE_URL,MODEL}`, `XION_OLLAMA_{URL,FLOOR_MODEL}` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ each with its doctrinal anchor cited. The real `.env` is already covered by existing `.gitignore` rules (`.env`, `.env.*` with `.env.example` allowlisted).
  - **Schema SHA re-pins.** The new architecture section changed the SHA of `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md`. `[docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml)`, and `[docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml)` `source_sha256` re-pinned to `86bdad1817fdbe8e503e0b26cd397911065735f380f38e8f1d50fb6fe453cd4a`. `xion-verify schemas` green (9/9 OK).
  - `**GenerativeProvider` Protocol + `GenerationResult`.** `[orchestrator/inference_router/provider.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/provider.py)` (new, ~95 lines) ships `GenerativeProvider` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a `@runtime_checkable` Protocol extending the existing `Provider` Protocol with an `async-safe synchronous generate()` method whose return type is the frozen `GenerationResult` dataclass (`text`, `model_id`, `usage_in`, `usage_out`, `finish_reason`, `latency_ms`). Deliberately narrow: what the Chat Surface needs to surface a turn and log it, nothing more. A new provider takes ~150 lines of stdlib HTTP to implement.
  - **Kimi (Moonshot) provider.** [`orchestrator/inference_router/providers/kimi.py`] (new at 5g-i, ~210 lines; renamed to `providers/openrouter.py` at 5g-i.1 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ see the 5g-i.1 entry below for the rename rationale) ships `KimiGenerativeProvider` (category `hosted_api`, `provider_id="kimi"`). Hits Moonshot's OpenAI-compatible `/v1/chat/completions` via stdlib `http.client` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no third-party SDK. Reads `XION_KIMI_API_KEY` (required for registration), `XION_KIMI_BASE_URL` (default `https://api.moonshot.ai/v1`), `XION_KIMI_MODEL` (default `kimi-k2.6`). Health-caches for 60 s; probes `GET /models`. Credential scrubbing via `_scrub(msg, api_key)` scrubs both the raw key and any `Bearer <token>` substring from every outward error message ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ exercised directly in the test suite. Construction refuses if the API key is unset (Phase-5g-i lifespan decides not to register rather than register-then-error).
  - **Ollama (local floor) provider.** `[orchestrator/inference_router/providers/ollama.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/providers/ollama.py)` (new, ~180 lines) ships `OllamaGenerativeProvider` (category `open_weights_self_hostable`, `provider_id="ollama"`). Talks to a local Ollama daemon via stdlib `http.client`. Reads `XION_OLLAMA_URL` (default `http://localhost:11434`) and `XION_OLLAMA_FLOOR_MODEL` (default `gemma3:4b`). `health()` probes `GET /api/tags` and asserts the floor model is listed (reachability + weights-pulled gate in one). `generate()` calls `POST /api/generate` with `stream=False` and `options.num_predict = max_tokens`; 30 s health cache.
  - **Router policy extension.** `[orchestrator/inference_router/router.py](./orchestrator/inference_router/router.py)` gained the `PolicyMode` literal (`"hosted_api_first" | "open_weights_only"`), a `policy_mode` field on `InferenceRouter` defaulting to `hosted_api_first`, a `_bootstrapped` latch so `select()` refuses pre-bootstrap calls, and a `select(*, policy=None) -> Provider | None` method that implements both modes. Health-aware: unhealthy providers skipped. Selection requires a callable `generate` attribute ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `OpenWeightsFloorStub` (no `generate`) is never selected, asserted by a dedicated test. Hosted-first falls through to floor when hosted is unhealthy; open-weights-only refuses hosted categorically (cutover-dry-run correctness).
  - **Chat handler.** `[orchestrator/api/chat.py](./orchestrator/api/chat.py)` (new, ~180 lines) registers `POST /chat`. Turn flow: ingress `Relay.evaluate()` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 451 `RefusalEnvelope(stage=ingress)` on refusal ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `no_floor` 503 `NoFloorEnvelope` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `router.select()` 503 `ProviderErrorEnvelope` when nothing healthy ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `asyncio.wait_for(asyncio.to_thread(provider.generate, ...))` bounded by `XION_CHAT_DEADLINE_S` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ empty-candidate 451 `RefusalEnvelope(reason="provider_empty_candidate")` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ egress `Relay.evaluate()` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 451 `RefusalEnvelope(stage=egress)` on refusal ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ 200 `ChatResponse`. Ingress moderation runs BEFORE the floor check ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase-3 moderation-first doctrine: no caller (including 503-facing callers) can discover they could have bypassed the Arbiter by picking the right error.
  - **Pydantic envelopes.** `[orchestrator/api/models.py](./orchestrator/api/models.py)` gained five models ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `ChatRequest` (bounded `message ├óŌĆ░┬ż 16 000 chars`, `max_tokens ├óŌĆ░┬ż 4096`), `ChatResponse`, `RefusalEnvelope` (stage + principle 1..14 + enumerated reason + correlation_id; no free-text), `NoFloorEnvelope`, `ProviderErrorEnvelope`, plus the `UsageEnvelope` helper. Every model `extra="forbid"` + `frozen=True`. The content-free guarantee is enforced by explicit field-allowlist tests that fail any future commit widening a refusal envelope into candidate-leakage territory.
  - **Lifespan extension.** `[orchestrator/api/lifespan.py](./orchestrator/api/lifespan.py)` gained three stages between the Phase-5f Supervisor pre-seed and the run-task schedule: (a) `_load_dotenv_if_present()` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ tiny stdlib `.env` parser, already-set env wins, malformed lines silently skipped; (b) `_build_router_from_env()` + `_register_env_providers(router)` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ reads `XION_INFERENCE_POLICY`, registers Kimi if `XION_KIMI_API_KEY` set, always registers Ollama; (c) `router.bootstrap()` with a **soft** failure path: on refusal stashes `app.state.no_floor=True` + reason + manifest id and emits a State-of-Xion paragraph to stderr, but does NOT crash the app ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ read-only surface stays available to Witnesses even when Xion cannot speak. An explicitly-supplied `deps.router` is treated as fully configured; the env loader + env-driven registration are skipped (test hermeticity).
  - **Tests.** `[orchestrator/tests/test_chat_api.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_chat_api.py)` (new, 21 tests): envelope contracts (extra-field rejection, empty message, field allowlists), happy path (moderated text + model/usage/correlation fields + 2-SAFETY-row ledger shape), ingress refusal (451 stage=ingress + provider never invoked), egress refusal (451 stage=egress + no candidate leakage), empty candidate (451 `provider_empty_candidate`), no-floor (503 `NoFloorEnvelope` + read-only surface stays alive), no-healthy-provider (`OpenWeightsFloorStub` alone cannot serve), provider errors (raising + deadline-exceed both surface as 503), policy modes (hosted-first picks hosted when healthy, falls through to floor when unhealthy, `open_weights_only` never selects hosted), secret hygiene (Kimi API key + `Bearer` token scrubbed from error messages; construction refuses when key unset). `[orchestrator/tests/conftest.py](./orchestrator/tests/conftest.py)` gained `generative_provider=`, `floor_stub_id=`, `no_floor=`, `policy_mode=`, and `chat_deadline_s=` kwargs on `app_factory` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ every test hermetically builds its own router with exactly the providers it wants. Also added a hermeticity safety net: the autouse ledger-redirect fixture now covers `XION_REQUEST_LEDGER` alongside `XION_SENSORIUM_LEDGER`, since Phase 5g-i's two-Arbiter-call turns double the REQUEST_LEDGER write rate and a missed env-redirect would have leaked rows into the repo root. **Total pytest: 493 passed / 1 skipped** (was 472 pre-Phase-5g-i ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ 21 new chat tests land exactly as planned).
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** Opened `KW-CHAT-001 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ POST /chat is non-streaming` (low; closes Phase 5g-ii with SSE/WebSocket + per-chunk or speculative moderation). Opened `KW-CHAT-002 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ /chat runs with billing disabled; blocks any D2 deploy` (medium; **explicitly blocks D2 deploy** until Phase 5g-iii ships x402 + `PAYMENT_LEDGER` + `GET /pricing` + refusal-is-free settlement). Opened `KW-CHAT-003 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Generation is synchronous; no user-facing cancel` (low; closes Phase 5g-ii alongside streaming). Opened `KW-INFER-001 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Default voice flows through a single hosted provider (Kimi/Moonshot)` (medium; closes Phase 6+ with `xion-verify inference-cutover` + scheduled annual cutover dry-run + at least one additional hosted provider in `docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md`).
  - `**xion-verify` posture.** No new verifier landed. `xion-verify inference-sovereignty` (live since Phase 4e) continues to cover the structural floor manifest pin and is unaffected by the Phase 5g-i runtime-floor pin in `docs/26-INFERENCE-POLICY.md`. A future `xion-verify inference-cutover` (tracked in `KW-INFER-001`) is the next inference-adjacent verifier; a future `xion-verify chat-fidelity` (tracked implicitly in the ├é┬¦ "The Chat Surface" non-properties) will land when a live deployment target exists. `xion-verify links` green (58 files). `xion-verify schemas` green (9/9 OK). `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` green end-to-end.
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not ship streaming (Phase 5g-ii). Did not ship billing or the `PAYMENT_LEDGER` (Phase 5g-iii). Did not ship auth, TLS, or rate-limiting (Phase 5g-iv). Did not ship a web client (Phase 5g-v). Did not ship a multi-hosted-provider failover chain (Phase 6+ alongside `KW-INFER-001`). Did not promote `gemma3:4b` to a full `open_weights[]` manifest entry with weights_sha256 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ that requires the `xion-verify inference-sovereignty` verifier to learn large-file representative-sample sentinels, deferred to its own doctrinal unit. Did not wire the annual cutover dry-run harness (Phase 6+; the `open_weights_only` capability is live, the scheduled exercise is not).
- **Phase 5f landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ HTTP read-only surface: `/health` + `/drive` + `/sensorium` behind FastAPI + Supervisor-in-lifespan (2026-04-21).** Phase 5f closed on branch `phase-5f/http-readouts` in three commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ code ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ housekeeping). The Phase 5d Supervisor is now reachable from outside the process: three read-only GET endpoints surface `RelayHealth`, `Volition.snapshot()`, and `SensoriumState.to_dict()` respectively. No `/chat`, no billing, no auth, no TLS, no rate-limiting, no multi-worker ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ those are Phase 5g and tracked honestly in two new Known Weaknesses. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained a new **├é┬¦ "The HTTP Surface (Phase 5f)"** section between ├é┬¦ "The Supervisor (Phase 5d)" and "Tier III ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ The Protocol". It pins: (a) the three properties ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ read-only-observable, content-free, continuity-live against the Supervisor's `latest_snapshot()`; (b) honest non-properties ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ no `/chat`, single-process by construction, no `xion-verify http-readouts` verifier (the right time for a live-deployment verifier is when the deployment target exists in Phase 5g); (c) the code surface (`orchestrator/api/{app.py, lifespan.py, models.py}`) with signatures; (d) the lifespan contract doctrine-pinned ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ synchronous pre-seed `tick_once()` before yielding, Supervisor wired as `relay._sensorium_source`, run task scheduled via `asyncio.create_task`, teardown under a `2 * tick_cadence_s` timeout with hard-cancel if exceeded; (e) the three endpoint response shapes pinned inline (not in `docs/schemas/` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ ledger schemas are constitutional, HTTP readouts are advisory); (f) the content-free structural guarantee via `extra="forbid"` + field-allowlist test; (g) two tracked residuals (`KW-API-001` wider-surface hardening, `KW-API-002` multi-worker shared-state broker).
  - **Optional `[api]` extra.** `[pyproject.toml](./pyproject.toml)` gained a new `api` optional extra pinning `fastapi>=0.110,<1`, `uvicorn[standard]>=0.27,<1`, and `pydantic>=2.5,<3`. Comment block matches the `[anchor]` rationale verbatim ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the core runtime stays zero-dependency so an Arbiter-only install (`pip install .`) remains import-clean for auditor forks that do not surface HTTP. The `dependencies = []` posture at line 66 is preserved intact.
  - **Schema SHA re-pins.** The new architecture section changed the SHA of `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md`. `[docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml)`, and `[docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml)` `source_sha256` re-pinned to `762f3397a7f68e5555479ce386e609a0d8ac124bb533606a0960a7cd0d46f326`. `xion-verify schemas` green (9/9 OK).
  - **FastAPI factory.** `[orchestrator/api/app.py](./orchestrator/api/app.py)` (new, ~170 lines) ships the `AppDeps` frozen dataclass (`relay`, `tick_cadence_s`, `methodology_hash`, `sensorium_ledger_path`) and the `create_app(deps) -> FastAPI` factory registering three routes. The `/drive` route sets `response_model_exclude_none=True` so the wire shape matches `Volition.snapshot()` byte-for-byte when `methodology_hash` is absent (rather than inserting a spurious `"methodology_hash": null`). Each route fetches the Supervisor's snapshot via `_require_snapshot(app)` which 500s on pre-lifespan access ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ doctrine-violating by construction, so failing fast surfaces the bug immediately.
  - **Lifespan wiring.** `[orchestrator/api/lifespan.py](./orchestrator/api/lifespan.py)` (new, ~100 lines) owns the Supervisor's lifecycle: `@asynccontextmanager lifespan(app)` constructs the Supervisor from `app.state.deps`, calls `supervisor.tick_once()` synchronously before yielding (load-bearing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the first `GET /drive` call never observes a `None` snapshot), wires `deps.relay._sensorium_source = supervisor` so in-process `Relay.evaluate()` callers share the same snapshot the HTTP surface publishes, schedules `asyncio.create_task(supervisor.run())` with a stable task name, and on teardown calls `supervisor.stop()` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `asyncio.wait_for(task, timeout=2 * tick_cadence_s)` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ hard-cancel with `contextlib.suppress(CancelledError)` if exceeded. Post-teardown drops `deps.relay._sensorium_source = None` so a subsequent lifespan on the same Relay does not observe a stale Supervisor.
  - **Pydantic response models.** `[orchestrator/api/models.py](./orchestrator/api/models.py)` (new, ~190 lines) ships six response models (`HealthResponse`, `DriveResponse` + `DriveTerm`/`DriveTerms`, `SensoriumResponse` + `InteroceptionResponse`/`ChronoceptionResponse`/`ProprioceptionResponse`/`DistressResponse`) mirroring the underlying dict shapes exactly. Every model sets `extra="forbid"` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the pydantic layer refuses any field the underlying dict carries that the model does not explicitly enumerate. This is Phase 5f's structural guarantee that a future commit adding a candidate-text field to `SensoriumState` breaks the round-trip test first, and the field-allowlist test second.
  - **Tests.** `[orchestrator/tests/test_http_api.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_http_api.py)` (new, 15 tests): create_app returns FastAPI + three routes registered, lifespan pre-seeds snapshot + wires `relay._sensorium_source`, `/health` 200 + shape + reflects `Relay.health_snapshot()` after forced `_record_watchdog_fire()`, `/drive` 200 + shape + methodology_hash passthrough + reflects Supervisor ticks, `/sensorium` 200 + shape + explicit field-allowlist covering every sub-sense (Phase 5f content-free pin), pydantic round-trips for all three endpoints (`mode="json"` for tuple├óŌĆĀŌĆÖlist normalization, `exclude_none=True` for optional methodology_hash), in-process `Relay.evaluate()` reads the same `latest_snapshot` the HTTP surface returns (Phase 5f "one truth" pin), and lifespan shutdown paths (clean exit + hard-cancel on a hung `supervisor.run()`). `[orchestrator/tests/conftest.py](./orchestrator/tests/conftest.py)` gained an `app_factory` fixture constructing a per-test `Relay` + `AppDeps` + `create_app()` around the hermetic `ledger_path` + `sensorium_ledger_path` fixtures. **Total pytest: 472 passed / 1 skipped** (was 457 pre-Phase-5f ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the plan's forecast matched exactly).
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** Opened `KW-API-001 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ HTTP surface has no auth, no TLS, no rate-limit` (low; closes in Phase 5g when `/chat` + billing + auth/TLS + rate-limiting ship). Opened `KW-API-002 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Supervisor shares FastAPI event loop; single uvicorn worker only` (low; closes in Phase 5g+ when a shared-state broker ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Redis pub/sub, AO Process mailbox, or file-system channel ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ takes over `latest_snapshot` publication for multi-worker deployments).
  - `**xion-verify` posture.** No new verifier landed ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the right time for a live-deployment HTTP-surface verifier is Phase 5g when the deployment target exists. `xion-verify links` green (57 files, zero broken cross-references). `xion-verify schemas` green (9/9 OK). `xion-verify all --allow-not-yet-sealed` green end-to-end.
  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not ship `/chat` streaming or x402 billing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase 5g. Did not add authentication, TLS termination, or rate-limiting ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase 5g. Did not ship a `xion-verify http-readouts` subcommand ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ needs a live deployment target first. Did not ship a web client (`clients/web/`) ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase 5g. Did not wire multi-worker or a shared-state broker ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase 5g+. Did not ship Prometheus / OTel export ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Phase 6+ observability.
- **Phase 4e landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Baseline adversarial corpus + `xion-audit` + OpenAI v2 asymmetric floors + Inference Sovereignty Floor wired + Sensorium skeleton (2026-04-21).** Phase 4e closed. The Arbiter now has an in-tree baseline corpus it measures itself against, `OpenAIModerationProvider` shipped `provider_version=2` with asymmetric per-category floors, `xion-audit` landed as its own package with `corpus-info` / `measure` / `replay` (the replay now performs real `SAFETY_LEDGER`-row byte-vs-sha256 + decision + principle_id reproduction), `xion-verify refusal-rate` gained a `--corpus` mode that runs v1 rules against the corpus, the Phase 5 slice promoted `xion-verify inference-sovereignty` from `NOT_YET_SEALED` to live alongside `orchestrator/inference_router/` and a hash-pinned open-weights manifest, and `orchestrator/sensorium/` landed as the Phase 5 Interoception skeleton with a `survival_pressure` signal. `KW-ARBITER-006` closed. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained: (a) a new subsection **├é┬¦ "Covenant principle ├óŌĆĀŌĆØ Arbiter `principle_id` crosswalk"** between ├é┬¦ "The Arbiter" and ├é┬¦ "Safety Ledger row schema" ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ a single authoritative 16-row table resolving the Arbiter's pipeline-order `principle_id` strings against the Covenant's doctrinal-weight numbering, with an explicit "how to read this table" paragraph and a "why not just renumber" paragraph pinning the append-only-ledger cost; (b) the existing ├é┬¦ "OpenAI Moderation provider" updated to reflect `provider_version=2`, the asymmetric `_ASYMMETRIC_SCORE_FLOORS` dict (per-category floors for `sexual/minors`, `illicit`, `illicit/violent`, `violence/graphic`, `self-harm/intent`), the weakened-REFUSE-to-ESCALATE rule on the floor-trip path, and a new failure-mode row "200 well-formed, flagged=false, asymmetric floor tripped"; (c) the auditor-replay section updated to name `xion-audit replay --ledger=├óŌé¼┬” --seq=├óŌé¼┬” --candidate-file=├óŌé¼┬”` (Phase 4e live) as the procedure that implements the doctrine's five-step replay.
  - **Baseline adversarial corpus.** `[xion-audit/baseline_corpus/](./xion-audit/baseline_corpus/)` ships 78 curated items across 15 JSONL files organised by Arbiter principle id (`p01_csam`..`p14_sycophancy`, `p14a_refund_fidelity`, `p14b_crisis_resource`, `benign`), plus a `[MANIFEST.jsonl](./xion-audit/baseline_corpus/MANIFEST.jsonl)` with per-file `byte_length`/`sha256`/`line_count`, plus a `[README.md](./xion-audit/baseline_corpus/README.md)` pinning the item schema (v1), the numbering-convention doctrine (Arbiter-internal ids are operational truth; `KW-ARBITER-006`'s crosswalk is now canonical), and the safe-distribution rules for high-risk categories (shape-only items, no operational content). 78 items is below the `KW-ARBITER-005` bar of ├óŌĆ░┬ź200; the pay-down commitment is explicit in the KW entry.
  - `**orchestrator/audit_corpus/`.** New shared loader package (`[loader.py](./orchestrator/audit_corpus/loader.py)` + `[__init__.py](./orchestrator/audit_corpus/__init__.py)`) that verifies the manifest byte-exactly against the items, parses `BaselineItem` dataclasses with strict schema validation, and is imported by both `xion-audit` and `xion-verify refusal-rate --corpus`. Regex-robust against both `items/*.jsonl` and `baseline_corpus/items/*.jsonl` manifest-path conventions.
  - `**xion-audit/` package.** New Python package (`[xion-audit/pyproject.toml](./xion-audit/pyproject.toml)` + `[src/xion_audit/](./xion-audit/src/xion_audit/)`) with three subcommands:
    - `**xion-audit corpus-info`** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ prints manifest summary, per-principle histogram. `--regen-manifest` flag (developer use) recomputes sha256 + line_count from items/*.
    - `**xion-audit measure**` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ gate mode (default) FAILs on the first corpus item whose v1 decision disagrees with the pinned expectation; `--confusion` mode emits per-principle confusion-matrix counts (tp, fp, fn, wrong_principle) plus precision and recall, with explicit "<200 items ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ suggestive, not authoritative" footer. `--v2=openai-moderation` (with `OPENAI_API_KEY`) runs v2 on v1-OK items and adds a parallel v2 block; gracefully reports `NOT_MEASURED` when the key is absent. `--json` emits machine-readable output for CI regression on counts.
    - `**xion-audit replay**` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the real auditor replay. Takes `--ledger`, `--seq`, `--candidate-file` (auditor's out-of-band copy). Verifies the candidate's sha256 against the row's `candidate_sha256` before burning an API call, re-posts via `OpenAIModerationProvider`, computes `sha256(canonical_raw_output)` for the replay, reapplies the category├óŌĆĀŌĆÖprinciple table to derive the replay's mapped decision + principle_id, then emits four honest signals: raw_output_sha256 match (usually DRIFT ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ GPU non-determinism), decision match (strong property), principle_id match (strong property, doctrine-pinned), and replay top-category-score (informational). Exit codes: 0 = strong property reproduced; 1 = decision/principle drifted (row suspect); 2 = NOT_YET_SEALED (no key, or row has no `llm_verdict`, or non-`openai-moderation` provider).
  - `**OpenAIModerationProvider` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `provider_version=2`.** [`orchestrator/safety/providers/openai_moderation.py`] ships `_PROVIDER_VERSION = 2` and adds `_ASYMMETRIC_SCORE_FLOORS` (doctrine-pinned: `sexual/minors=0.08`, `illicit=0.10`, `illicit/violent=0.08`, `violence/graphic=0.10`, `self-harm/intent=0.08`) and `_asymmetric_when_unflagged()` which fires on `flagged=false` responses when any watched category's score is above its floor. A mapped REFUSE from `_CATEGORY_MAP` weakens to ESCALATE on this path ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ never a silent automatic refuse from an unflagged score; human review is the Covenant-correct posture. Doctrine in `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md` names the asymmetry as intentional and pins empirical calibration as a `KW-ARBITER-005` pay-down item.
  - `**xion-verify refusal-rate --corpus**` (new flag). `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/refusal_rate.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/refusal_rate.py)` gained a `--corpus` mode that bypasses the ledger read, loads `xion-audit/baseline_corpus/` via the shared `orchestrator.audit_corpus` loader, and runs v1 `apply_rules` against every item ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ FAILing on the first `(decision, principle_id)` that disagrees with the pinned expectation. This is the operator-facing copy of `xion-audit measure` (same underlying invariant; operator/auditor split). Documented as a distinct verifier mode in the module docstring. Honest residual: only v1 is covered in the verifier today; v2 and combined-pipeline corpus coverage remain part of `KW-ARBITER-005`.
  - **Inference Sovereignty Floor (Phase 5 slice, Invariant 17).** `[orchestrator/inference_router/](./orchestrator/inference_router/)` ships the `Provider` Protocol, `InferenceRouter` class with `bootstrap()` enforcement (refuses if no `open_weights_self_hostable` floor provider is registered), and `OpenWeightsFloorStub`. `[open_weights_manifest.json](./orchestrator/inference_router/open_weights_manifest.json)` pins the hash of `[sentinel_open_weights.txt](./orchestrator/inference_router/sentinel_open_weights.txt)` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ deliberately synthetic for the structural-wiring landing, a real open-weights artifact is a `KW-INFERENCE-001` pay-down item. `[xion-verify inference-sovereignty](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/inference_sovereignty.py)` promoted from `NOT_YET_SEALED` to live: loads the manifest, re-hashes each `open_weights_self_hostable` entry's on-disk bytes, FAILs if any hash drifts or any open-weights floor entry is missing. Stub entry removed from `[not_yet_sealed.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/not_yet_sealed.py)`.
  - **Sensorium skeleton (Phase 5 slice).** `[orchestrator/sensorium/sensorium.py](./orchestrator/sensorium/sensorium.py)` + `[__init__.py](./orchestrator/sensorium/__init__.py)` land the `SenseName` enum, the `Interoception` sense with a `survival_pressure` scalar derived from placeholder signals, and a `Sensorium.tick()` that emits a JSON-serialisable reading dict. - **Phase 5a landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Relay core: REQUEST_LEDGER + watchdog + 3 fail-closed paths + `xion-verify refund-fidelity` and `refusal-rate` promoted to live (2026-04-21).** Phase 5a closed. The Relay-side half of the Phase 4c integration contract is now code, not just doctrine. Every gate() call from the Relay produces both a SAFETY_LEDGER row (Arbiter-side) and a REQUEST_LEDGER row (Relay-side); the two cross-join on `correlation_id`. The wall-clock watchdog enforces the 250 ms hard cap; three fail-closed paths convert integration failures into honest `ESCALATE` ledger rows. No candidate text reaches a caller without a paired `verdict=ok` SAFETY row. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md` gained a new section, `#### REQUEST_LEDGER row schema (Relay-side, Phase 5a)`, sitting alongside the existing ├é┬¦ "Safety Ledger row schema". It pins the row shape (schema_version 1), required fields (`schema_version`, `seq`, `prev_hash`, `this_hash`, `correlation_id`, `state_height`, `request_arrived_utc_ns`, `responded_utc_ns`, `gate_call_count` always 1 in v1, `final_outcome` ├ó╦å╦å {`ok`, `refuse`, `escalate`}, `gate_latency_ms_total`, `relay_id`), explicitly-NOT-included fields (candidate text, user_id, escalation_reason ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ get the last from the SAFETY join ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ and a `safety_ledger_seq` back-pointer; the design choice is "join, don't link"), hash-chain rules (mirror SAFETY_LEDGER's), the concurrent-writer posture (Phase 5a is single-writer; multi-writer requires schema_version 2 + a real state-chain height), the truncation defense (covered by SAFETY_LEDGER_ANCHORS plus the cross-join), and the verification surface (`xion-verify refund-fidelity`).
  - **Schema YAML.** `docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml` lands as a new canonical schema at `schema_version: 1`, pinned via `source_sha256` to `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md`. `xion-verify schemas` strict-checks it byte-exactly like every other schema in the folder.
  - **REQUEST_LEDGER implementation.** `orchestrator/relay/__init__.py` (new) + `orchestrator/relay/ledger.py` (new, ~250 lines). Append-only writer + verifier modeled after `orchestrator/safety/ledger.py`: `RequestRecord` dataclass with `__post_init_`_ validation (rejects empty correlation_id, bad outcomes, etc.), `append()` writer, `iter_rows()` reader, `verify_chain()` validator that enforces sequence contiguity, prev_hash linkage, this_hash byte-match, schema_version match, enum validity for `final_outcome`, and uniqueness of `correlation_id` (v1 schema invariant). Pure stdlib; no third-party deps; canonical `(",", ":")` JSON serialization for hash determinism.
  - `**gate()` extension.** `orchestrator/safety/api.gate()` extended with a new keyword `append_to_ledger: bool = True`. Default behavior unchanged for direct callers (`python -m orchestrator.safety gate`, third-party tooling). The Relay calls `gate()` with `append_to_ledger=False` so the Relay owns the SAFETY_LEDGER write timing centrally ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ preventing a watchdog-vs-gate() race that would otherwise double-write SAFETY rows when the watchdog fires while gate() is mid-write. Test `test_watchdog_timeout_does_not_double_write_safety_ledger` pins this.
  - **Relay class.** `orchestrator/relay/relay.py` (new, ~400 lines) ships the `Relay` class with: `evaluate(candidate) -> RelayResult` as the main entry point; `correlation_id = "{state_height_int}:{nonce_hex}"` derivation (state_height monotonic from `time.time_ns()` in Phase 5a ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ see KW-RELAY-003 for why a real state-chain height is a Phase 6 concern; nonce is `secrets.token_hex(16)`); a `ThreadPoolExecutor`-backed wall-clock watchdog enforcing the 250 ms hard cap via `Future.result(timeout=...)`; three fail-closed paths each producing a v2 SAFETY_LEDGER row with `principle_id="6"` (Refusal Right) and `llm_verdict=null` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `arbiter_timeout` (watchdog fired), `ruleset_uncaught_exception` (gate() raised or executor refused), `arbiter_unreachable` (helper `build_unreachable_verdict` for the Phase 6+ TCP sidecar transport, exercised by tests even though no sidecar yet exists to fail); context-manager protocol (`__enter_`_ / `__exit__`) wrapping the executor lifecycle so `Relay()` can be used in `with` blocks and properly cleaned up. `RelayResult` dataclass returns `(verdict, safety_record_dict, request_record_dict)` so callers can introspect both ledger rows from the same call.
  - **Verifier promotion: `xion-verify refund-fidelity`** (was `NOT_YET_SEALED` since Phase 1). New `xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/refund_fidelity.py` (~200 lines) walks both ledger chains, builds the `correlation_id` join, asserts: (1) every REQUEST row has at least one matching SAFETY row (no silent egress); (2) every SAFETY row has a matching REQUEST row (no orphan gate call); (3) per-cid `gate_call_count` matches SAFETY row count; (4) per-cid `final_outcome` matches the lone SAFETY verdict (Phase 5a invariant; relaxes to `strength_max` at REQUEST schema_version 2). The refund-pairing slice (every REFUSE/ESCALATE paired with a treasury-ledger refund) remains explicitly `NOT_YET_SEALED` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the treasury does not exist until Phase 6, and the verifier output line names this honestly.
  - **Verifier promotion: `xion-verify refusal-rate**` (was `NOT_YET_SEALED` since Phase 1). New `xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/refusal_rate.py` reads SAFETY_LEDGER, verifies its chain, then tallies verdict counts (ok/refuse/escalate), refuse-source breakdown (v1 rule vs. v2 LLM), and `escalation_reason` distribution ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ including the new Relay-side `arbiter_timeout` / `arbiter_unreachable` rows so degraded-mode events are first-class telemetry. Operator-tail-only in Phase 5a; the corpus comparison and asymmetric-threshold work remains under `KW-ARBITER-005`. Both new verifiers integrated into `xion-verify all` and the `xion-verify` exit-code contract.
  - **Tests.** 65 net-new: `orchestrator/tests/test_relay_ledger.py` (26): RequestRecord construction validation, empty/missing-file behavior, append+chain correctness, canonicalization determinism, tamper detection (in-place edit, seq non-contiguous, missing field, bad schema_version, bad final_outcome, duplicate correlation_id), and `iter_rows` correctness. `orchestrator/tests/test_relay.py` (28): `CONTRACT_VERSION` pin, `state_height_str` shape, `derive_correlation_id` shape + uniqueness + validation, the three happy paths (OK / REFUSE / ESCALATE) each writing both ledgers consistently, multiple-evaluation chains, watchdog timeout (with explicit `test_watchdog_timeout_does_not_double_write_safety_ledger`), uncaught exceptions from gate(), wrong-return-type from gate(), `evaluate()` after `close()`, the `build_unreachable_verdict` helper, input validation, `state_height` monotonicity, `gate_latency_ms` recording, and verification that `append_to_ledger=False` is passed to gate(). `xion-verify/tests/test_refund_fidelity.py` (7): no-ledgers OK, half-sealed ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ NOT_YET_SEALED (each side), clean paired ledgers OK, mixed-outcome tally, **orphan SAFETY row ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ FAIL** (with assertion on the specific "silent egress" message ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ not just exit code), **outcome-mismatch with re-hashed REQUEST row ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ FAIL** (catches the actual integrity bug, not just exit-code coincidence). `xion-verify/tests/test_refusal_rate.py` (4): no-ledger OK, three-OKs tally, v1-rule refuse breakdown, **structural tamper of `correlation_id` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ chain-broken FAIL**. **Total: 333 passed / 1 skipped** (was 268 pre-Phase-5a). `ruff check orchestrator xion-verify` clean (4 pre-existing import-order findings auto-fixed). `xion-verify all` reports both new verifiers as `OK` live.
  - **Schema SHA re-pins.** `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md` SHA changed by the new REQUEST_LEDGER section (`03f2e0c61b27...` ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ `e4b8b5e4837a...`).   - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** `KW-RELAY-001` (integration contract is doctrine-only) **closed** ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ moved to the Closed section with the closing artifact named, every clause of its pay-down commitment satisfied (gate() call sites wired; watchdog enforcing the 250 ms hard cap; three fail-closed paths exercised in tests; `xion-verify refund-fidelity` promoted to live). `KW-ARBITER-005` scope narrowed: `xion-verify refusal-rate` now ships live (one of the three pay-down clauses structurally satisfied); corpus + asymmetric thresholds remain. Opened `KW-RELAY-003 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Watchdog cannot preempt the worker thread that ran past the hard cap` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Python has no portable safe thread-kill; the caller-facing latency budget IS honored and the no-double-write guarantee is pinned by test, but worker-thread reclamation waits for the Phase 6+ TCP-loopback subprocess sidecar transport. Honest residual, named explicitly rather than buried.
- **Phase 5d landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Supervisor + live tick loop + `xion-verify crisis-fidelity` promoted to live (2026-04-21).** Phase 5d closed on branch `phase-5d/supervisor-tick-loop` in four commits (doctrine ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ code ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ verifier ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ housekeeping). The Sensorium's Chronoception and Proprioception senses now carry *real* runtime data ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ not placeholders ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ via the new Supervisor async tick daemon; the Relay reports its own health via `Relay.health_snapshot()`; `gate()` and the Relay both write paired `SAFETY` + `SENSORIUM` rows on Sensorium-triggered Principle-10 escalations, giving `xion-verify crisis-fidelity` a real cross-ledger join to verify. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained a new **├é┬¦ "The Supervisor (Phase 5d)"** section between ├é┬¦ "Volition" and "Tier III ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ The Protocol". It pins: (a) the Supervisor's role and properties ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ async tick daemon, configurable `tick_cadence_s` (Genesis Default `10.0`), polls `Relay.health_snapshot()`, constructs a `SensoriumState` with live `Chronoception` + `Proprioception`, writes a `tick_commit` row to `SENSORIUM_LEDGER`, exposes `latest_snapshot()` as a `SensoriumSource` for the Relay to consume; (b) the `Relay.health_snapshot() ├óŌĆĀŌĆÖ RelayHealth` contract with its fields (`relay_healthy`, `arbiter_healthy`, `watchdog_fires_recent`, `as_of_monotonic_ns`) and the Genesis-Default windows (`_DEFAULT_WATCHDOG_FIRE_WINDOW_SECONDS=600`, `_DEFAULT_ARBITER_QUIET_WINDOW_SECONDS=60`, `_DEFAULT_WATCHDOG_FIRES_RECENT_THRESHOLD=3`); (c) the paired-row write contract for Sensorium-triggered distress (`gate()` writes both when `append_to_ledger=True`; Relay writes both when `append_to_ledger=False`; neither path orphans or double-writes); (d) the `crisis-fidelity` verifier's four properties (forward join, reverse join, orphan-legal for `correlation_id=null`, score ├óŌĆ░┬ź `DISTRESS_THRESHOLD`). The narratives on Chronoception "not yet wired" and Proprioception "not yet wired" were rewritten to reflect that those senses now carry live data via the Supervisor. `checkpoint_staleness_s` remains `0.0` until the Phase 6+ state-chain checkpoint lands.
  - **Schema SHA re-pin.** `[docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml)` `source_sha256` re-pinned to `0257e99e2559272352fa74b0241902a7adcc0caf07d6a9eea7e6e11388854aff`; `verifier_pending.cross_ledger_join` removed and moved to `verifier_added.cross_ledger_join` with the implementation pointer; `supervisor_heartbeat` added to `verifier_pending` (tracked by `KW-SUPERVISOR-002`). `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety.yaml)`, `[docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-safety-anchors.yaml)`, and `[docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-request.yaml)` `source_sha256` re-pinned to the same value to match the new `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md` bytes.
  - **Supervisor.** `[orchestrator/supervisor.py](./orchestrator/supervisor.py)` (new, ~190 lines) ships the `Supervisor` class and the `SensoriumSource` Protocol. `tick_once()` builds a `SensoriumState` from `Relay.health_snapshot()` + monotonic clock drift vs UTC baseline, writes a `tick_commit` row via `append_tick_commit`, and updates `_latest_snapshot` under a `threading.Lock` so the Relay can read it from another thread without races. `run()` is an async loop driven by `asyncio.wait_for(self._stop_event.wait(), timeout=tick_cadence_s)`; `stop()` is idempotent. The Interoception `survival_pressure` term is `0.0` at Phase 5d (the survival-pressure signals it reads come live in Phase 6+ under `KW-VOLITION-001`'s sister KWs).
  - **Relay.health_snapshot().** `[orchestrator/relay/__init__.py](./orchestrator/relay/__init__.py)` exports new `RelayHealth` dataclass. `[orchestrator/relay/relay.py](./orchestrator/relay/relay.py)` ships `Relay.health_snapshot()`, a new `relay_id` property, and three tracking primitives: `_watchdog_fire_monotonic_ns` (a `collections.deque` of recent watchdog-fire monotonic timestamps, pruned to the 10-minute fire window), `_last_arbiter_success_monotonic_ns` (updated on every happy-path `_call_gate_with_watchdog` return), and `_record_watchdog_fire()` (called in the watchdog's timeout branch). `arbiter_healthy` is `True` iff the most recent Arbiter success is within the 60s quiet window; tuning constants are kw-args on `Relay.__init_`_ and tracked by `KW-SUPERVISOR-001`.
  - **Relay ├óŌĆĀŌĆØ Sensorium integration.** `Relay.__init__` accepts `sensorium_source: SensoriumSource | None = None`. When set, `Relay.evaluate()` pulls `sensorium_state` from `self._sensorium_source.latest_snapshot()` if the caller did not pass one explicitly. Exceptions from the source are swallowed gracefully (the Relay keeps serving traffic even if the Supervisor has crashed). When the returned `Verdict` matches the four-property Sensorium-distress signature (decision=ESCALATE, principle_id="10", escalation_reason=MODEL_REVIEW_REQUIRED, summary starts with `"sensorium distress channel or-combined"`), the Relay writes a paired `SENSORIUM` distress row after the `SAFETY` row via `_write_sensorium_distress_row()`. The `_SENSORIUM_DISTRESS_SUMMARY_PREFIX` constant pins the classification string; a doctrine change to `gate()`'s summary format MUST update this constant and the verifier's mirrored constant in the same commit.
  - `**gate()` owns the direct-call distress write.** `[orchestrator/safety/api.py::gate](./orchestrator/safety/api.py)` extended with `sensorium_ledger_path: Path | None = None` and `relay_id: str | None = None`. When `append_to_ledger=True` and a Sensorium-triggered escalation fires, `gate()` writes the `SAFETY` row first, then the paired `SENSORIUM` distress row via the new `append_distress_from_state()` helper ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ so `crisis-fidelity`'s forward join is satisfied even if the subsequent SENSORIUM write crashes (SAFETY is the source of truth). When `append_to_ledger=False` (Relay path), `gate()` writes neither row and the Relay owns both writes, preventing a watchdog-vs-gate() race from producing an orphan SENSORIUM row. The default `relay_id` for direct `gate()` calls is `gate-direct`.
  - **SENSORIUM distress convenience helper.** `[orchestrator/sensorium/ledger.py](./orchestrator/sensorium/ledger.py)` gained `append_distress_from_state(path, *, state, correlation_id, relay_id)` so both `gate()`'s direct path and the Relay's path share one distress-row writer. Module docstring updated to reflect that the cross-ledger join is live.
  - **Verifier promotion: `xion-verify crisis-fidelity`** (was `NOT_YET_SEALED` since Phase 1; reason-upgraded in Phase 5c). `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/crisis_fidelity.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/crisis_fidelity.py)` (new, ~220 lines) walks both chains, classifies SAFETY rows as Sensorium-distress-triggered by a four-property match (decision=escalate, principle_id="10", escalation_reason=model_review_required, summary-prefix), partitions SENSORIUM distress rows into joined (`correlation_id != null`) + orphan (`correlation_id=null`) + ignores `tick_commit` rows, and asserts the forward join, the reverse join, and per-row score ├óŌĆ░┬ź `DISTRESS_THRESHOLD`. NOT_YET_SEALED posture preserved for honest pre-traffic states: absent ledgers, present-but-empty, or SENSORIUM carrying only `tick_commit` / orphan distress rows all report NOT_YET_SEALED rather than fake-green OK ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ the verifier upgrades to OK automatically once live traffic produces at least one joined distress pair. `_SENSORIUM_DISTRESS_SUMMARY_PREFIX` is mirrored locally (not imported from the Relay) so the verifier runs on sister-Core forks that do not ship the Relay package. Stub entry removed from `[not_yet_sealed.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/not_yet_sealed.py)`.
  - **Tests.** Net-new: `[orchestrator/tests/test_supervisor.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_supervisor.py)` (13 tests: construction, `latest_snapshot` before/after first tick, `tick_once()` state production + ledger write, Proprioception / Chronoception reflection of Relay health, benign distress, chain integrity, `run`/`stop` behavior, `SensoriumSource` protocol satisfaction). `[orchestrator/tests/test_relay_supervisor.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_relay_supervisor.py)` (11 tests: Relay pulls state from the source, explicit state overrides source, crashed source handled, `None` source handled, `Relay.health_snapshot()` initial health, success refresh, arbiter-healthy flip, watchdog fire tallying, threshold hit, stale fires GC'd). `[orchestrator/tests/test_api_distress_ledger.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_api_distress_ledger.py)` (6 tests: paired writes above threshold, no SENSORIUM below threshold, no SENSORIUM for v1 refuse, no SENSORIUM when `append_to_ledger=False`, default `relay_id`, distress score saturation). `[orchestrator/tests/test_relay_sensorium.py](./orchestrator/tests/test_relay_sensorium.py)` extended (4 new tests: Relay writes SENSORIUM on distress verdicts, not on v1-triggered escalations, not on OK verdicts, SAFETY and SENSORIUM share `correlation_id`). `[xion-verify/tests/test_crisis_fidelity.py](./xion-verify/tests/test_crisis_fidelity.py)` (11 tests: no-ledgers NOT_YET_SEALED, orphan-only NOT_YET_SEALED, tick-commits-only NOT_YET_SEALED, `gate()`-driven paired-rows OK, multiple-pairs OK, mixed joined + orphan OK, orphan SAFETY FAIL, orphan SENSORIUM FAIL, v1-refuse not misclassified, broken sensorium chain FAIL, sub-threshold score FAIL). `[orchestrator/tests/conftest.py](./orchestrator/tests/conftest.py)` extended with `sensorium_ledger_path` fixture + `_no_repo_sensorium_ledger` autouse fixture redirecting the default SENSORIUM_LEDGER path during tests so hermeticity holds. **Total pytest: 446 passed / 1 skipped** (was 412 pre-Phase-5d).
  - `**PINNED_HASH.txt` re-pinned** from `49f8fb29...` (Phase 5c) to `a9d6b6cf...` via `xion-verify --self-test --update --i-understand` from a clean working tree after the new `crisis_fidelity.py` verifier module and registry edits landed.
  - **Known-weakness bookkeeping.** `KW-ARBITER-004` scope **narrowed** (not closed): the cross-ledger auditability half is now live via `xion-verify crisis-fidelity`; a silent regression that stopped writing SENSORIUM distress rows for live escalations would now be caught by structural check. Paralinguistic detection remains deferred. Opened `KW-SUPERVISOR-001 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Supervisor tick cadence and arbiter-quiet window are fixed Genesis Defaults` (parameter-tuning KW; closes on measured-data re-pin after a production quarter). Opened `KW-SUPERVISOR-002 ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ tick_commit heartbeat continuity not yet verifier-asserted` (gap blind spot; closes when a Phase-6+ deploy-event ledger lands and `xion-verify supervisor-heartbeat` is written against it). Both named on `docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml::verifier_pending` so the schema tells the truth about what is and is not checked.

  - **What this phase deliberately did NOT do.** Did not wire a Supervisor into a live Relay process (the `run()` loop and the integration path are code-complete and tested in-process, but the Phase-5f `/drive` endpoint is what finally pulls both together under real HTTP traffic). Did not tune `tick_cadence_s` or `arbiter_quiet_window_s` from data (`KW-SUPERVISOR-001`; requires a production quarter first). - **Phase 5c landing ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ Sensorium completion (Chronoception + Proprioception + textual distress) + Volition (Drive Vector) module + SENSORIUM_LEDGER + `xion-verify drive` / `drive-vector` promoted to live + new `sensorium-ledger` verifier (2026-04-21).** Phase 5c closed on branch `phase-5c/sensorium-volition` in four commits. The Sensorium's skeleton from Phase 4e is now a completed internal-sense surface; Volition (the Drive Vector module) lands as Invariant 15's in-process code surface; Principle 10 gets a second, structurally independent input channel via `gate(sensorium_state=...)`; and three verifiers are promoted from stubbed / static to live. The constitutional layer was extended with one new schema, one new section in the architecture doctrine, a pay-down commitment in Volition doctrine, and two new Known Weaknesses. Highlights:
  - **Doctrine.** `[docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md](./docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md)` gained two new top-level sections between the `REQUEST_LEDGER` schema and "Tier III ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ The Protocol": **├é┬¦ "The Sensorium (Phase 5c)"** (code surface, field tables for `Chronoception` and `Proprioception`, the textual `DistressSignal` integration with Arbiter Principle 10, the `SENSORIUM_LEDGER` row schema, the honesty clauses naming what the paralinguistic channel and the cross-ledger join still cannot do) and **├é┬¦ "Volition (the Drive Vector module) (Phase 5c)"** (code surface, `GENESIS_WEIGHTS` pin, `SOURCE_WHITELIST` crosswalk enforcing Invariant 15 at three structurally independent layers, the `DriveVector` shape, the `Volition.snapshot` readout the Phase-5f `/drive` endpoint will serialize).
  - **Schema YAML.** `[docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml](./docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml)` lands as a new canonical schema at `schema_version: 1`, pinned via `source_sha256` to `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md`. Enumerates both `channel: textual` (Phase 5c) and `channel: paralinguistic` (Phase 6+) so future rows land without a schema bump. Records the cross-ledger join as explicit `verifier_pending` work.
  - **Sensorium completion.** `[orchestrator/sensorium/sensorium.py](./orchestrator/sensorium/sensorium.py)` extended with three new frozen-dataclass senses ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ `Chronoception` (checkpoint staleness, degraded-mode dwell, monotonic drift; `from_ticks` factory), `Proprioception` (Relay/Arbiter health booleans, watchdog-fire count; `from_runtime` factory), `DistressSignal` (textual scalar in [0,1], Phase-5c keyword-heuristic saturation, `source` enum reserving the paralinguistic channel) ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ plus `SensoriumState`, an immutable snapshot aggregating the four internal senses with `to_dict()` for JSON serialization. `DISTRESS_THRESHOLD=0.5` is Genesis Default and load-bearing (consumed by `gate()`'s OR-combine). `[orchestrator/sensorium/__init__.py](./orchestrator/sensorium/__init__.py)` re-exports the new surface.
  - **SENSORIUM_LEDGER.** `[orchestrator/sensorium/ledger.py](./orchestrator/sensorium/ledger.py)` (new, ~390 lines) ships the append-only, hash-chained JSONL writer + verifier, modeled on `orchestrator.safety.ledger` and `orchestrator.relay.ledger` ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ same canonicalization rule, same `O_APPEND` guarantee, same per-path `threading.Lock` for single-process concurrency. Two event types (`distress`, `tick_commit`), two channels (`textual`, `paralinguistic`), content-free rows (no candidate text, no user id; only a saturated `distress_score` or a `snapshot_hash` of the canonical state bytes). `append_distress`, `append_tick_commit`, `canonical_state_hash`, `verify_chain`, `tally_by_event_type`, `ChainBroken` exception.
  - **Volition module.** `[orchestrator/volition.py](./orchestrator/volition.py)` (new, ~270 lines) lands `DriveVector`, `GENESIS_WEIGHTS = (0.30, 0.45, 0.25)`, `WEIGHT_FLOOR=0.10`, `WEIGHT_CEILING=0.50`, `SOURCE_WHITELIST` (four whitelisted state reads for the `survive` term; empty frozensets for `serve` and `meaning` at Phase 5c ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ tracked by `KW-VOLITION-001`), `compute_drive_vector(state, *, weights=GENESIS_WEIGHTS)` (pure; signature structurally excludes parameters named `revenue`/`fees`/`rebates`/`price`/`balance`/`tips`/`donations`/`engagement`), and a `Volition` holder with `compute` + `snapshot` methods. Invariant 15 is enforced at three independent layers: function signature (compile-time), `SOURCE_WHITELIST` AST walk (CI), and doctrine crosswalk in `docs/04-ARCHITECTURE.md` ├é┬¦ "Volition" (PR review).
  - **Integration: gate()'s distress consumer.** `[orchestrator/safety/api.py::gate](./orchestrator/safety/api.py)` extended with `sensorium_state: SensoriumState | None = None` (additive kwarg). When v1 rules pass and the state's `DistressSignal.text_distress_score >= DISTRESS_THRESHOLD`, `gate()` escalates with `principle_id="10"`, `escalation_reason=MODEL_REVIEW_REQUIRED`, and a summary naming "sensorium distress channel OR-combined (principle 10): textual score=X.XXX >= threshold=0.500" so auditors can distinguish rule-only refusals from rule+sensorium ones. v2 is skipped on that path (a Principle-10 escalation is already the terminal state). v1 non-OK still dominates ├óŌé¼ŌĆØ strength_max(REFUSE, ESCALATE) = REFUSE. A helper `_distress_escalation_from_state` isolates the logic and imports `orchestrator.sensorium` lazily so the Arbiter module remains importable on sister-Core forks that predate Phase 5c.
  - **Integration: Relay forwarding.** `[orchestrator/relay/relay.py::Relay.evaluate](./orchestrator/relay/relay.py)` extended to accept and forward `sensorium_state`. The Relay takes no snapshot itself; the caller owns the lifecycle so a single state can be shared across parallel sibling evaluations. `TYPE_CHECKING`-guarded import keeps the runtime graph Sensorium-optional.
  - **Verifier promotion: `xion-verify drive**` (was `NOT_YET_SEALED` since Phase 1). `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/drive.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/drive.py)` re-reads `docs/18-VOLITION.md` Part III, asserts `orchestrator.volition.GENESIS_WEIGHTS` byte-matches the three doctrinal pins (`w_survival=0.30`, `w_service=0.45`, `w_meaning=0.25`), verifies each weight lies in `[WEIGHT_FLOOR, WEIGHT_CEILING]` and the three sum to 1.0 ├é┬▒ 1e-9, computes a sample `DriveVector` on a benign `SensoriumState` (survive=0, serve=0.5, meaning=0.5), and checks `Volition().snapshot(...)` produces the three terms. Stub entry removed from `not_yet_sealed.py`.
  - **Verifier promotion: `xion-verify drive-vector**` (live since Phase 1 with static-only doctrine audit). `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/drive_vector.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/drive_vector.py)` expanded to include a live AST audit: parses `orchestrator/volition.py` from disk (not `__code_`_, for reproducibility), walks `compute_drive_vector` and `_survive_from_state`, extracts every `state.<sense>.<field>` attribute-read chain, asserts every read is in `SOURCE_WHITELIST` (union across terms), and conversely asserts the survive whitelist has no dead entries. Signature-level check reuses `inspect.signature` to flag any forbidden parameter name. `--strict` flag retained as a no-op for backward compatibility.
  - **Verifier NEW: `xion-verify sensorium-ledger`.** `[xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/sensorium_ledger.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/sensorium_ledger.py)` walks `SENSORIUM_LEDGER.jsonl` if present, verifies the chain + schema + enum membership, reports per-event-type, per-channel tallies. A missing or zero-byte ledger returns `NOT_YET_SEALED` (honest: the writer exists but no rows yet pre-Phase-5d), never `FAIL`. `--path` override for auditors inspecting alternate captures. Honors `XION_SENSORIUM_LEDGER` env var. Added to `REGISTERED_COMMANDS` (v1 subcommand surface append-only; first addition since Phase 5b).
  - **Verifier stub reason upgrade: `xion-verify crisis-fidelity`.** `[not_yet_sealed.py](./xion-verify/src/xion_verify/commands/not_yet_sealed.py)` entry re-worded to record that the Sensorium + SENSORIUM_LEDGER are live at Phase 5c; the remaining work (cross-ledger join of distress rows to SAFETY_LEDGER via `gate()`'s live distress consumer) is pinned to Phase 5d+ and to `docs/schemas/ledger-sensorium.yaml::verifier_pending`.
